Current Commentary

The Seriousness of Customs Duty Evasion 7

— End

According to the national budget for the 24th year of the Republic, China's customs revenue is listed as 326,361,400 yuan, accounting for 43% of the total recurring revenue of 761,970,199 yuan. If we compare it to the debt servicing expenses of 274,803,279 yuan, it accounts for 84% of the customs revenue. It is clear that customs duties occupy a crucial position in China's finances. The surplus or deficit of tax revenue is of great importance. In recent years, all industries have been in decline, and the agricultural villages have gone bankrupt, so the volume of imports and exports is not as prosperous as before. The practice of tax evasion has become even more prevalent. Initially, merchants would only smuggle and conceal goods, hoping to reduce the burden. For example, Article 1, Section 2 of the Provisional Regulations for the Revised Import Tariff of the Ministry of Finance stipulates that if a merchant refuses to present a genuine invoice and does not provide a reasonable explanation that satisfies the customs, the merchant has no right to protest against the amount of tax levied by the customs on the goods. This is intended to prevent tax concealment. Although tax concealment is detrimental to tax revenue, it is not the same as tax evasion. Since the outbreak of war in the north, smuggling in Qinhuangdao and Yushugou has suddenly increased. Recently, there has even been the organization of "Cooperative Trading Stations" specializing in smuggling. Goods smuggled out of the customs are silver, silver dollars, and Central Bank and Bank of Communications notes. Goods smuggled into the customs are linen, sugar, artificial silk, etc. The smugglers are organized and armed. When they encounter customs anti-smuggling personnel, they use force to resist. In one instance, they were caught smuggling artificial silk, resulting in a customs officer being beaten and left for dead. On its way back from an anti-smuggling mission on the waters off Yantai, a customs patrol ship was detained by Japanese military police on a pretext. Yantai and Dalian are separated by only a narrow strip of water. Qingdao has the latent power for smuggling. It has become customary. If it obstructs their actions, they will inevitably be jealous and resentful. Although the customs in Xiamen is working hard to combat smuggling, smuggling groups are organized, have backgrounds, and have bodyguards. Customs ships are met with gunfire when they pursue smugglers. From January 1 to September 19 of this year, only a little more than 4,900 bags of imported foreign sugar were imported, which is a small number. They were all sold in Zhangzhou. Xiamen does not produce sugar and has no reserves, so where do the more than 2,000 bags of sugar consumed each month come from? It is known that they are smuggled. There are 500 Japanese Taiwanese people in Shantou. They collect foreign rice, bean cakes, and artificial silk from Guangdong Province and sell them at a special tax. The various trade donation taxes on controlled white sugar, cement, and fertilizer are heavy, and prices are expensive. Taiwanese people see that there is profit to be made, so they purchase large quantities of rice, beans, and bean cakes and dump them in Shantou without paying taxes, so the prices are low. The inventories of various industries have been greatly affected.

The customs duties of China are mostly used as collateral for internal and external debts and indemnities. If tax revenue is insufficient, how can it fulfill its obligations? If one party undermines its tax revenue and the other party orders it to reorganize its old debts, China, although trustworthy, does not have the magic touch to turn lead into gold. Therefore, preventing smuggling is not only a problem that the Chinese authorities should focus on, but also other countries that are related to this and want to improve their foreign relations with China should also provide assistance.

British Ambassador Visits Japanese Vice Minister; Shigemitsu Says Japan Pays Attention to the Overall Situation 8

(Tokyo) When British Ambassador to Japan Clive visited Vice Minister Shigemitsu yesterday, Shigemitsu told him that Japan could not favor one side or the other in the Italian-Abyssinian war. The Italian-Abyssinian war is currently being considered by the League of Nations, and Japan cannot express its attitude on this matter. This war can be described as a European war. League of Nations members, including Britain, should take a stand first. Shigemitsu said at the end that Japan is paying attention to the overall situation and is very concerned. (5th Reuters Telegram)

War Affects Various Industries; Dollar Steamship Lines Do Not Dock in Hong Kong 9

(New York) The Dollar Steamship Company yesterday issued an order that its ships should not go to Italian commercial ports. Today, "Dollar" issued an explanation, saying that it was because war risk insurance premiums were too high. Yesterday, insurance companies had increased the war risk insurance premiums for voyages to Italian ports from 52.5 cents to one dollar. (4th National Telegram)

(London) The Lloyd's insurance company and insurance brokers are currently busy answering a large number of inquiries about war risk insurance premiums. War risk insurance premiums for Europe in the next three months are mostly quoted at £15 15s per £100. (5th Reuters Telegram)

(London) The war risk insurance premium quoted by Lloyd's Insurance Company today is 75%, indicating that the probability of a European civil war before the end of the year is 3 to 1. (4th European Telegram)

(London) The British Steamship Company told Reuters today that the company's ships do not intend to avoid the Suez Canal route and sail around the Cape of Good Hope in South Africa, because there is currently no need to avoid the route. The company has a special mail contract, so it must have government permission before it can change its route. (5th Reuters Telegram)

Alexandria, Export merchants here have been receiving urgent requests to purchase Egyptian cotton in the past two days, fearing that a blockade will occur and disrupt the supply of essential raw materials needed for the manufacture of military supplies such as automobile tires, tents, and military uniforms. British exporters are unwilling to ship cotton to Italy because Italian importers are unwilling to pay for the goods in advance. However, Italian exporters are still shipping cotton to Italy. Today, two Italian ships carrying 4,000 bales of cotton sailed from here to Italy. (5th Reuters Telegram)

Naval Cooperation Issue: France's Positive Reply to Britain; Requests Army and Air Force Cooperation as Well; and Prior Consultation Necessary 10

(London) The French Ambassador to Britain, Corbin, delivered the French government's reply to the Foreign Office this morning. According to our correspondent, the French reply is of a positive nature, and its content is as follows: (1) France hopes that Britain will accept mutual obligations; (2) The cooperation between the two countries should not be limited to the navy alone, but should also include the army and air force; (3) Britain and France should also cooperate to deal with acts of aggression by non-League of Nations member states; (4) Mutual consultation should take place before mutual assistance is implemented. In addition, France raised several questions as follows: (1) Should mutual assistance between Britain and France not be limited to dealing with countries that violate the League of Nations Covenant? Is Britain prepared to assist France if there are violations of the Locarno Pact? (2) Will Britain consult with France before implementing various preventive measures so that these measures are not mistaken as provocative? (3) Regarding mutual assistance plans, can Britain technically agree on a method in advance? (Havas dispatch, 5th)

(Paris) The British government recently inquired of France what attitude it would take if the British fleet in the Mediterranean were attacked. Regarding this question, the French government has now provided a reply, which was delivered to the French Ambassador to Britain, Corbin, tonight for transmission to the British government. It is reported that the gist of the reply is that if an incident occurs in the future due to the execution of certain actions, and such actions have been consulted with France in advance and are endorsed by France, then France will accept all its responsibilities. Furthermore, France is willing for the French navy to assist Britain, but at the same time, Britain must also allow that if the same situation occurs on the European continent in the future, Britain should also provide the same level of assistance to France. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Laval's Policies Receive Confidence of French Cabinet; Will Meet with Italian Representative Again 11

(Paris) The French cabinet meeting has instructed Foreign Minister Laval not to approve the implementation of severe sanctions against Italy. An Associated Press reporter learned today from authoritative sources that France is only willing to participate in very mild economic and financial sanctions and opposes any military sanctions. A statement was issued after the cabinet meeting, stating that the cabinet has just approved Foreign Minister Laval's official statements in the League of Nations and has decided on his future position in Geneva. From this, it can be seen that the cabinet members unanimously trust Laval. (National News Agency dispatch, 5th)

(Paris) The cabinet meeting this afternoon discussed the diplomatic situation and unanimously decided on the following two points: (1) No military sanctions will be taken against the aggressor nation; (2) France is prepared to participate in economic pressure on the aggressor nation, such as refusing loans, prohibiting the transport of munitions and raw materials needed for military industries to the aggressor nation, and completely prohibiting the purchase of goods from the aggressor nation. As for a blockade, it should be regarded as a military measure, but if the blockade is implemented in a gradual manner so that various efforts can be used at the same time to seek a cessation of armed conflict, then France is also prepared to give it a try. In short, the main outline of French policy is to respect the obligations it has undertaken to the League of Nations, but it should take the recommendations unanimously passed by the League of Nations Administrative Council as its maximum limit. It is also reported that the Italian representative Aloisi is scheduled to arrive in Geneva tomorrow, at which time French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval will make proposals to Aloisi. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

(Paris) With the full support of the French Premier Laval, it has been firmly decided that France must carry through to the end and fulfill its obligations under the League of Nations Covenant. At the same time, France will continue to strive for a resolution of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute so as not to affect European peace. It is reported that Laval is now prepared to support: (1) declaring Italy as an aggressor nation, and the procedures for sanctions under the League of Nations Covenant should be followed; (2) refusing credit and loans to Italy and prohibiting the import of raw materials into Italy; (3) banning the import of Italian goods into France. It is reported that the sanctions steps discussed by Laval and British cabinet member Eden also include lifting the ban on the supply of military supplies to Ethiopia and France and Britain jointly blockading to prevent Italian military supplies from entering East Africa, etc. However, Laval has not asked the cabinet to allow him to carry out this plan, in anticipation of which France may ultimately agree to lift the ban on the supply of military supplies to Ethiopia. However, the talk of a blockade will cause serious opposition from various political parties now demanding neutrality. The French cabinet held an important meeting this afternoon to study the general situation, which lasted for three hours and only ended at 6:10 pm, after which a communiqué was issued. It is said that the cabinet has approved the government's reply to Britain's inquiry as to what attitude France will take if the British fleet in the Mediterranean is suddenly attacked by the Italian fleet. It is reported that this reply will be delivered to London tonight, stating that if Italian ships attack the British fleet in the Mediterranean before the League of Nations implements sanctions, then France is prepared to support Britain, but Britain must also give the same guarantee that if the same incident occurs in the future and affects France, Britain should also assist France. Laval reported on the international situation and the matters to be discussed by the League of Nations in great detail at the cabinet meeting. The cabinet unanimously supported Laval's position to be taken in Geneva and expressed complete trust in Laval. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(Paris) Although the cabinet yesterday approved the principles of Anglo-French cooperation and Foreign Minister Laval's continued freedom to deal with contingencies in Geneva, the cabinet members unanimously insisted on forceful reservations. Responsible parties stated today that the extent to which France is willing to bear is to join in prohibiting the export of munitions and raw materials for munitions and the extension of loans. France does not want to join in blockading Italy, nor does it want to sever diplomatic and commercial relations, and it is even less willing to join in any plans that could lead to war. Before starting for Geneva, Laval assured the cabinet members that he would act cautiously and would never involve France in any plans unless Britain gave a firm guarantee to assist France in the same way in the event of a Franco-German war. Before his departure, Laval issued a statement urging the people to remain calm and end party strife in order to cope with the world crisis. As can be seen from this, newspapers here indicate that if Foreign Minister Laval approves military sanctions, France is bound to have a civil war. A large number of monarchist youths marched through the streets today, shouting "Down with sanctions!" Members of the French National Social Party posted slogans everywhere saying "We don't want the League of Nations' troops." (National Society News dispatch, 5th)

Roosevelt Immediately Orders Blocking of Arms Exports; Recognizes Italy and Ethiopia as Already at War 12

(Washington) According to sources close to the government, President Roosevelt will soon recognize that Italy and Ethiopia are already at war. Before dusk, the President will order the blocking of arms shipments to belligerent countries. (National News Agency dispatch, 5th)

(Washington) The State Department today promulgated the arms manufacturing and export regulations in the recently passed Neutrality Act. This move is particularly noteworthy given the recent tense situation in Europe. However, it is not known whether arms exports will be blocked. (National News Agency dispatch, 5th)

(Washington) Senior State Department officials stated today that the United States' attitude towards the Italo-Ethiopian issue will follow the lead of the League of Nations, that is, to gradually impose an arms embargo on belligerent countries, or to declare the United States' position on the state of war in Africa or Europe. It is deeply felt here that an arms embargo can only have a moral impact. According to the State Department, the only real help that the United States can provide in this crisis is in the moral realm. Most observers here believe that if the United States announces a ban, it will only include weapons and ammunition; other military supplies, such as food, copper, and cotton, will not be included in the ban. There is much speculation in Europe about what the consequences will be if the United States still supplies raw materials and food to Italy after the League of Nations implements economic sanctions against Italy. It is believed here that even if the United States supports collective European sanctions, these items cannot be prohibited from export. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Senator Nye of the Republican Party of South Dakota told an Associated Press reporter today that if the United States cooperates with Britain and France to implement economic sanctions against Italy, it will be drawn into the whirlpool. Nye is the chairman of the Senate Munitions Investigation Committee and is an extreme advocate of American neutrality in Congress. Nye continued to say that there is only one way to maintain neutrality, and that is that we should not unilaterally sanction one of the belligerent countries. If sanctions are necessary, then we should treat the belligerent countries equally, without discrimination. Ninety-nine percent of Americans are determined to avoid war, but a few weeks of propaganda can easily change their attitude. We should be wary of the fact that the events of 1914 may be repeated today. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

(Washington) The U.S. Chargé d'Affaires in Ethiopia, Engert, reported to the State Department today that he had ordered three American women and six children to take the train to British Somaliland to take refuge. These women and children are all family members of Adventist missionaries. Engert also said that the Ethiopian Emperor had promised to protect American nationals within the country, and British officials also asked American nationals to take refuge in the British Consulate. Secretary of State Hull declined to comment on this report. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Atlantic City, New York. The president of the American Federation of Labor, Green, declared today that no matter what kind of sudden event occurs abroad, American workers demand that the government strictly adhere to neutrality. Green's statement was made to the American Building Trades Department, which represents the views of American workers nationwide. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

(Rome) The American consulate here has issued a warning to Italian medical students residing in Rome who were born in the United States, stating that if they volunteer to serve in the Italian army, they will lose their American citizenship. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Observations from London; War Inevitable; European Peace Hanging by a Thread 13

(London) Observers here today generally believe that as the African war progresses, European peace is also hanging by a thread. In view of the concentration of naval and air forces and the laying of mines in the Mediterranean, there is also a possibility of danger before the League of Nations can pass military sanctions, because a touch-and-go situation is enough to draw Italy into the whirlpool of European war. The news that Italian ports are laying mines and that large ocean liners are not docking in Italian ports is enough to prove this danger. It is reported that other shipping companies have also ordered their ships to avoid the entire Mediterranean Sea. The increase in war risk insurance premiums is enough to prove that all of Europe deeply fears that the Italo-Ethiopian conflict may spread. Premier Mussolini declared to the Associated Press reporters that the solution to the Abyssinian problem must be decisive and thorough. At that time, observers of the European situation believed that Mussolini was not exaggerating. The news received today is even more proof of this matter. Therefore, the news from Geneva tomorrow may be even more unfavorable. The current thorny issue in Europe is how to stop the war in Abyssinia so that it does not spread to Europe. It is generally believed that economic sanctions alone are definitely not enough to slightly suppress Mussolini's ambition. Judging from today's situation, the League of Nations Administrative Council will clearly rule that Italy is an aggressor nation, so that Article 16 of the Covenant will automatically take effect. After that, the Administrative Council should decide the nature and scope of sanctions, as well as the method of implementation. It is now believed here that France will support the sanctions policy, and the first step will be to adopt economic sanctions. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Hawaii: America's First Line of Defense; Statement by U.S. Secretary of War 14

Honolulu. Secretary of War Dern stated in a speech here today that the Hawaiian Islands are America's first line of defense in wartime. The hope for permanent peace has gradually disappeared in the past few months, so sacrificing America's shipbuilding program will not remedy the overall situation. Dern is passing through this place on his way to Manila to attend the inauguration ceremony of the autonomous government. On the way, he will also stay briefly in Japan, Shanghai, and Hong Kong. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Italy and Spain Sign Trade Agreement 15

(Rome) The trade agreement between Italy and Spain was signed today. The agreement aims to regulate mutual import trade on the basis of concessions and conveniences. It is believed that this agreement will go beyond the ordinary conveniences of the most-favored-nation clause, and it is believed that Spain will not participate if the League of Nations decides to implement sanctions against Italy. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Current Status of World Gold and Silver Circulation 16

(New York) The gold shipped to New York yesterday is said to be worth a total of $38,600,000, of which $29,700,000 was shipped from France, $5,300,000 from the United Kingdom, $2,100,000 from Canada, and $510,000 from India. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(New York) In the week ending September 27, U.S. silver imports decreased significantly, with a decrease valued at $14,195,000. The total value of imports for that week was $1,828,000, of which $878,000 came from Mexico, $244,000 from Peru, $239,000 from Canada, $188,000 from India, $75,000 from Hong Kong, $70,000 from Honduras, $65,000 from Russia, and $49,000 from Chile. The total value of silver imports for the previous week was $16,023,000. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(London) In the week ending October 2, the quantity of British silver exports was almost the same as in the previous week, while the quantity of imports decreased significantly. The total value of silver exports for this week was £1,469,000, of which £1,436,000 was shipped to the United States. The total value of silver exports in the previous week was £1,472,000, of which £1,459,000 was shipped to the United States. The total quantity of silver imports for this week was £2,356,000, a decrease of £2,128,000 compared to the previous week, of which £1,829,000 came from Hong Kong, £305,000 from Japan, £103,000 from Soviet Russia, and £44,000 from India. The total quantity of imports in the previous week was £4,484,000. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(London) In the week ending October 2, British gold exports decreased, while imports also decreased slightly. The total value of exports was £6,780,000, a decrease of £2,943,000 compared to the previous week, of which £4,941,000 was shipped to the United States, £1,512,000 to Norway, £220,000 to Switzerland, £74,000 to the Netherlands, and £6,000 to France. The total value of exports in the previous week was £9,723,000. The total quantity of gold imports for this week was £2,101,000, of which £2,108,000 came from Africa, £420,000 from the Netherlands, £328,000 from India, £123,000 from France, £46,000 from Switzerland, and £40,000 from Venezuela. The total quantity of imports in the previous week was £3,305,000. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening price was low by 2 pounds. Later, due to multiple parties closing out, the price continued to fall, but the market situation turned sluggish, and the price did not change much after that.

Rubber

New York: Due to the rise in foreign demand, the opening price rose by 7 pounds, but the market situation turned sluggish later.

Securities

Yao Bay Entire Town Tragically Submerged; Yi River Suddenly Breached, Destroying More Than 500 Houses; Entire City Surrounded by Water; All Fields Turned into Lakes 22

(Zhenjiang) The Yi River in Yao Bay breached for more than ten zhang on the morning of the 5th, destroying more than 100 houses inside and outside the East Fang Gate. The entire town was submerged. The people climbed onto roofs and trees. The scene was extremely miserable. Luo Ma Lake rose another foot, diverting water into Liu Tang, and the disaster situation in Dongguan and Shu Counties worsened. County Magistrate Zhang of Suqian led 50,000 people to rescue the situation, hoping to reduce the disaster area. In order to reduce the disaster area in the coastal counties, the Provincial Government decided to dig through the Yanhai River and the Burning Incense River near Nancheng in Guanyun County, recruiting 2,000 to 3,000 laborers and setting a deadline of seven days to connect them. The Cenchi River and Zhou Port will also be dredged, recruiting 20,000 laborers and setting a deadline of half a month to complete the work, so that they can flow smoothly into the sea in the future. (Special telegram, 5th)

(Qingjiangpu) The Yi River South Bank in Yao Bay, which had been assaulted by water from the breach in Da Yushu, Pi County, was breached for about 30 zhang at ten o'clock at night on the third day in spite of the residents' efforts which proved unequal to the strength of the water after a month of the embankment's gradually cracking. More than 100 houses were destroyed and there were numerous casualties among people and livestock since it happened at night when it was too late to flee. Fortunately, the town had made preparations, so there were fewer deaths except for the houses. According to the Fifth District Office, Suqian County Magistrate Zhang Naifan reported on the 4th to the Thunder Flood Prevention Office, detailing the process and asking for ways to stop the breach. (Special telegram, 5th)

(Xuzhou) The floodwaters of the Yun River in Yao Bay rose sharply, flowing rapidly and backflowing into the Qi River, causing the Yi River to suddenly breach on the evening of the 3rd, flooding a very wide area. The river was more than ten zhang deep. Yao Bay faces the Yun River and has the Yi River behind it. The entire city was surrounded by water. Only the streets with the highest elevation still stood on the water surface, and all the fields were turned into lakes. (Special telegram, 5th)

(Qingjiangpu) Affected by the Yi River dyke break, the waters in the central Yun River have risen sharply for days, with only seven stones remaining out of the Qingjiang sluicegate (meaning more than 23 are submerged). (Special telegram, 5th)

West Embankment of Suqian Canal Breached in Multiple Locations 23

(Qingjiangpu) The situation of the west embankment of the Suqian Canal between Benjie Huangdun and Zhongyun had long been dangerous. Due to the efforts of Suqian officials and people to protect it, it finally breached in four places: Sujiafang, Liujia Store, Zhoujia Zhage, and Lijia Zhage, ranging in width from ten to twenty zhang. County Magistrate Zhang of Suqian telegrammed the Flood Control Office to report. (Special telegram, 5th)

(Qingjiangpu) Feng Dan, Director of the Huai-Pi Section Engineering Office, because the new and old embankment of the Suqian Canal were breached section by section, and the central Yun River and Huangdun Lake were connected into one, the water in the canal rose sharply by a foot. It sent a telegram to Section Chief Tang of the Second Flood Prevention Section stationed in Suqian on the 4th, urging him to lead the workmen and help protect and prepare materials to protect the dyke of the Zahe River. (Special telegram, 5th)

(Qingjiangpu) The western embankment of the Suqian Canal was cracked by the waters of Huangdun Lake, and the openings of the breach was located at many points. The Central Canal was discharged into the Lake. By the 4th, the water of Luo Ma Lake east of the East dyke had risen sharply by more than ten zhang. At the same time, the water of Zhao Wang Lake also rose. Since the water could not be discharged for a short period of time, it had risen gradually from the east dyke. The situation in the area around the first, second, and third bays was very dangerous. (Special telegram, 5th)

The Embankments on the West Bank of the Guanyun Salt River Have Completely Collapsed 24

(Xuzhou) Seaside News: Continuous strong winds and heavy rains have caused surging tides. The embankments built on the west bank of the Salt River in Guanyun County, from Dayi Mountain in the south to Banpu in the north and Zhongzheng Houtan in the west, have been completely breached by the Yellow River water, which was blocked by the tides and had nowhere to drain. The townships west of the river have all been submerged, causing severe damage with autumn crops washed away and houses collapsing. (Fifth Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Seaside News: To prevent Yellow River water from entering the city, Xinpu has mobilized a large number of laborers to build embankments along the Salt River and dredge the silted-up Longwei River to facilitate drainage. Donghai is also rushing to build the Lintou dike to protect the urban area. Zhangyun, anticipating strong northeasterly winds, is actively collecting materials for flood prevention and dividing them into piles at the six city gates for storage. Although the water level in the areas of Tuntang and Pei County is stable, the water in Datun has risen sharply, and the Xiaohubei dike has been destroyed in many places by strong winds. Reinforcements are being added to prevent danger. (Fifth Dispatch)

Dangerous Conditions Also Arise on the East Bank of the Huaiyin Canal Embankment 25

(Qingjiangpu) The old "Three Hundred and Sixty Zhang Project" on the east bank of the canal near Shuangjin Gate in the Fourth District of Huaiyin experienced a sudden surge in canal water yesterday due to continuous westerly winds, revealing dangerous conditions. The township head of that area, Xia Fengzhi, immediately rushed to the city to report. At the same time, residents along the Bianmin River in Yuanji Village in the Third District, Guitang, Linqiao Yusha in the Fourth District, and the Fifth District panicked. The county government has ordered the district chiefs of the aforementioned districts to immediately summon the township heads to mobilize laborers for emergency repairs. (Fifth Dispatch)

Yellow River Water Seizes the Canal Route 26

(Qingjiangpu) Yellow River water has seized the canal route. One stream entered the main channel from Hanzhuang at the Weishan Lake mouth, and another stream broke through the Lanjiaba breach in the west dike of Weishan Lake, entering the Xutang canal mouth and passing through the Bulao Fangting rivers, inundating Tang Songshanxi's new dike into Huangdun Lake, breaking through the western dike of the central canal and entering the canal. The area above Mao'erwo in Pizhou is a continuous expanse of rivers and lakes, navigable directly to Dongzhuang. This is the situation of the Yellow River breach, where the western and central canal mainstreams have been seized. East of the canal, the breach at Dayushu in Pizhou County has the most turbulent flow. Because it is blocked by the southern dike of the Yi River, most of the Yellow River water still follows the Yi River and enters the canal from the Zhulou Dam. Therefore, although the eastern dike of the canal in Pizhou has collapsed, the downstream ice conditions in the central canal are still rising due to this. (Fifth Dispatch)

Observations on a Trip West: Talks with Zhang Qun, Chairman of Hubei Province 83

After arriving in Hankou on the afternoon of the 22nd with Mr. Wang Jiyuan, the reporter crossed the river to Wuchang the next morning and visited Mr. Ma Manfei and Mr. Sun Jiyi of the Provincial Government Secretariat. At 5 pm on the 24th, upon the introduction of Feng Ruozhi, the reporter paid a visit to Zhang Yuejun, Chairman of the Provincial Government, and had a long conversation for over an hour. The main points of his talk are recorded as follows:

The reporter stated that the purpose of this trip was to observe the general situation in Sichuan, so he first asked Mr. Zhang to describe the recent situation in Sichuan. Zhang said that the obstacles to progress in Sichuan are gradually being removed, and everything is gradually getting on the right track. He deeply hopes that foreign investment will flow in in the future, which will make all construction easier. He then inquired about the recent situation in Hubei Province, the policy direction, and the situation in Wuhan. Zhang replied that since arriving in Hubei, it had been six months, and he had focused on (1) educating the people, (2) organizing the people, and (3) cultivating the people's productive capacity, aiming to achieve the goal of "everyone using their talents and the land yielding its benefits." The difficulty is that Hubei Province has not recovered since the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), and this year it has suffered another huge flood. The area affected by the disaster is even greater than that of the 20th year of the Republic. Forty-nine of the province's seventy counties were affected by the flood, and another seven counties were affected by the drought, with a total of more than seven million victims. Under these circumstances, it is necessary to economize in all aspects and raise funds to help the victims. Due to financial constraints, many construction projects have not been fully implemented. At present, the provincial government's monthly expenditure is only 80,000 yuan. The salaries of the officials were already very low, and have recently been reduced by another 10%, making life even more difficult. Therefore, those who want to work in officialdom flock to the capital, followed by provinces such as Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which are relatively affluent. Those who come to Hubei Province to work must have a spirit of sacrifice, so there are very few. As for the commercial situation in Wuhan, it is very difficult. After the flood of the 20th year of the Republic, many small and medium-sized shops were washed away. Those that exist now are relatively strong, so from a superficial point of view, the economic downturn is very deep.

Regarding the cause of this year's flood in Hubei Province, some say it was due to the flooding of the Yangtze River, some say it was due to flash floods, and some say it was due to the sudden rise of the Han River. Opinions vary. According to Zhang's discussion of the causes of this flood and the strategies for flood control and disaster relief, he said that the reason why this year's disaster in Hubei Province was so serious was due to the simultaneous rise of the Yangtze River and the Han River. To control floods, it is necessary to find solutions upstream of the Yangtze River and the Han River. As the saying goes, "The Yangtze River is the benefit of Sichuan, but the disaster of Chu." Judging from the situation in the past four years, this is very credible. However, the fundamental solution to the flood disaster in Hubei Province cannot be achieved by Hubei Province alone, and requires overall planning, design, and implementation by the central government. The most important thing is to imitate the flood control methods of the Mississippi River in the United States, and artificially set up water storage areas upstream, so that the water in the downstream areas will not rise suddenly, and the rise will not be too high. At present, Wuhan's commerce is very exhausted due to the impact of the global economic downturn, and the agricultural economy has also been greatly affected. It is expected that this winter, urban commerce and rural economy will be more difficult than in previous years. Therefore, in terms of disaster relief, we can only focus on work relief, and winter relief is especially important and must be planned in advance. Hubei Province has limited financial resources, and we deeply hope that the central government will provide subsidies.

He also asked whether it was possible to promote industry in Hubei Province in the near future. Zhang said that China is an agricultural country, and if China wants to modernize, it is impossible without increasing industry. However, Hubei Province does not have many mineral resources, but the cotton industry has always been developed. Therefore, his personal economic policy was originally to first promote cotton planting and the cotton textile industry, so that both farmers and workers can benefit. Unfortunately, the yarn factories in Hankou are currently affected by the dumping of foreign goods, and three of the four factories have been shut down one after another. Even if we want to promote the yarn industry, it is not easy. He expressed deep emotion. Finally, he reiterated that transportation and water conservancy are the prerequisites for all material construction. If transportation is not developed, industry and commerce cannot be promoted. If water conservancy is not emphasized, floods will occur frequently, and the construction of the rural economy will not be solid. Therefore, if China wants to develop, it needs specialized talent in transportation and water conservancy in the future.

Page 10

Tianjin: The East Asia Economic Association: Extremely Broad Scope, Many Founders are Politicians; the Declaration Vigorously States that Cooperation Between China and Japan is Necessary 84

Tianjin Correspondence · Niu Chuanshan · Shen Tongwu · Liu Xiangye · The East Asia Economic Association, organized by various people, has recently been sponsored by the Japanese military and merged into the North China Economic Relief Committee, organized by Gao Lingyu, to expand the organization and apply to the Tianjin Social Bureau to forward it to the Tianjin Municipal Government for filing, and is calling for a private economic cooperation organization, gathering a large number of past politicians, warlords, lawyers, and industrialists in Tianjin. There are as many as sixty founders, and the inaugural meeting will be held soon. As for the North China Economic Association, which Gong Xinzhan and others plan to organize, it is not clear whether it will continue to proceed. The names of the preparatory members and founders, the charter, and the declaration of the association are recorded as follows:

(2) Founders: Niu Chuanshan, Gao Jue, Zheng Wanzhan, Chen Zemin, Xu Fosu, Shen Tongwu, Huang Jicheng, Liu Xiangye, Chen Dingyuan, Chen Leshan, Cai Linshu, Cheng Hanqing, Li Songchen, Xu Junmian, Xu Shanbo, Huang Yabo, Zhou Lijun, Li Pang, Liu Shaokun, Hui Yuxu, Zhou Yufu, Zhang Yimeng, Zhang Bowu, Song Xiangqing, Yang Aitang, Gao Chongyuan, Kong Zepu, Rao Yonghong, Mengkedeleger, Damilinzapu, Huang Xiling, Guo Yinyuan, Zhang Xiaoyu, Dong Xicheng, Yang Rongmao, Huang Dao, Tao Xiang, Diao Huiyuan, Wang Shihong, Wang Yiwen, Fan Xiren, Chen Wenzhao, Tan Daonan, Yan Hanmei, Sun Hongyi, Li Hexian, Miao Xingcun, Song Feiqing, Yao Guozhen, Chen Zengliang, Xu Jieping, Wu Aichen, Tang Shixing, Liu Enyuan, Peng Jie, Zhang Shaoshu, Chang Mianzhai, Li Xiangzhou, Li Hongyue, Gao Peishu, Gan Baoxin, Liu Zhuoran, Zhu Yiren, Zhao Songqin, Yang Yuzhong, Zhao Hongfu, Wang Runzhen, Wang Peiyuan, Yang Younong, Chen Xunxu, Fu Binyu, Wu Tongen.

Charter

Article 1: This association is named the East Asia Economic Association. Article 2: The purpose of this association is to seek the development of the East Asian economy and the development of various industries. Article 3: Anyone who agrees with the purpose of this association and is introduced by two or more members and approved by the Board of Directors may become a member of this association. Article 4: This association will have a general headquarters in Tianjin and branches in various places. Article 5: The duties of this association are as follows: (1) Matters related to various industrial surveys; (2) Matters related to the establishment of various industries; (3) Matters related to investment liaison; (4) Matters related to the introduction of technical personnel; (5) Matters related to resolving local emotional issues; (6) Matters related to promoting joint venture benefits; (7) Other financial matters. Article 6: The General Assembly of Members of this Association shall be convened by the Board of Directors, but if one-fifth or more of the members consider it necessary to hold a meeting, they may request the Board of Directors to convene it. Article 7: When the General Assembly of Members of this Association is held, one of the Standing Directors shall serve as the chairman. Article 8: The General Assembly of Members of this Association shall make decisions by a majority vote of those present. Article 9: Matters decided by the General Assembly of Members shall be executed by the Board of Directors separately. Article 10: This association shall have fifteen directors, who shall be elected by the General Assembly of Members, and nine standing directors, who shall be elected by the Board of Directors. This association shall have an unlimited number of honorary directors, who shall be elected by the Board of Directors. Article 11: The Board of Directors represents this association, but it must be valid with the approval of more than half of the directors present. The Standing Board of Directors represents the Board of Directors and performs its duties with the signatures of three or more people. Article 11: This association shall establish the following departments to carry out the various matters in Article 5: (1) General Affairs Department, which manages the association's documents, compilation, accounting, general affairs, publicity, public relations, and matters not belonging to other departments; (2) Survey Department, which manages the matters that this association should investigate; (3) Design Department, which manages the matters that this association should design. Article 13: Each department shall have one director, two deputy directors, and an unlimited number of staff members. The director shall be recommended by the Standing Board of Directors, and the staff members shall be recommended by the director and deputy directors. The director and deputy directors of each department shall carry out their duties under the direction of the Standing Board of Directors. Article 14: This association may invite well-known figures from home and abroad who have economic experience or specialized knowledge to hold symposiums and invite them to express their opinions and exchange knowledge. Article 15: The detailed rules for the Board of Directors, the Standing Board of Directors, and the departments of this association shall be determined separately by the Board of Directors. Article 16: The expenses of this association shall be freely determined or separately raised by the members. Article 17: These articles of association shall be implemented after being filed with the government.

Declaration

The declaration of the East Asia Economic Association states: "Land is what nourishes people. The secret of natural selection and survival of the fittest has been established, and it is increasingly evident that no one does not seek survival. In recent times, the theory of opening doors has filled the world, and cunning acquisition and forceful seizure, based on the weak being preyed upon by the strong, are not permitted by the public, but closing doors and rejecting others, even if it is enough to protect precious jade, is also not allowed by the situation. Being able to understand this meaning is enough to talk about the current world economic competition. However, the definition of a country has its own indestructible definition in social science. Those who advocate internationalism without borders are trying to destroy other people's countries in the name of doctrines, deceiving others for their own benefit, and causing every country on earth to be in danger. Examining the origin of this theory, it is nothing more than taking the remnants of "the capitalist system will inevitably collapse, and the socialist system will inevitably rise instead," and advocating and promoting it in the hope of smashing the existing economic organizations of various countries in the world and proving that their doctrine can be promoted quickly. It is strange that the capitalist countries of today are digging their own graves, such as tariff wars, production recovery, and currency inflation. All these measures are aimed at harming others and benefiting oneself, even to the point of squeezing the blood and sweat of allied countries to pay for the cost of military expansion. If glory is not restored, collapse will occur immediately. Isn't this just causing the enemy to be emboldened and the loved ones to be chilled? Originally, production relations occur between humans, and they are becoming increasingly profound internationally. Therefore, these relations between countries are not only unavoidable but also need to be well combined. The productivity and production relations of Country A and Country B should correspond to each other and cooperate together, and their economic organization will be healthy. It is hoped that international economic relations will be extremely intricate and complex, so it is appropriate to adopt the group economic policies that are popular today, expand them, and choose those with contiguous lands, the same race, and similar lifestyles and cultures, and unite them on the principle of equality and mutual benefit. Seek only growth, do not engage in squeezing. In this way, in terms of national survival and development, there will be no internal pressure, and it will be possible to respond to trends from the outside. The self-existence and self-determination of the East Asian nations are also justified, but the fact that they are fighting each other has led to them being at the mercy of others. It is like a family fighting for property. At first, they are fighting for food, then they are stripped of their clothes, and neighbors are invading. The family is destroyed and will not stop until they are all dead. Then, looking back at the internal strife, is it really something that cannot be stopped? The reason why we believe that East Asian economic relations must cooperate is one reason. World peace is threatened again, and none of them do not stem from the struggle of economic groups. The horizontal and vertical exclusions between European countries, the conflicts of emerging forces on the Danube, the old reefs that exist in the Balkan Peninsula, and the current tension between Italy and Asia, are said to be political deductions that are stimulated to form. It is better to say that they are economic aggressions that are forced into this. The final scene of America's recovery policy and the Soviet Union's second five-year plan is not difficult to reveal. Then, East Asia is an excellent market, and how can competition be an exception? However, whether the economic situation in East Asia is stable depends on World War II and is not superficial. However, as far as China is concerned, its vast land and abundant resources are in urgent need of development, and its cheap labor is far beyond the reach of other countries. If all industries are fully developed, productivity will inevitably increase, and purchasing power will also increase accordingly. If it is used to inject into the world market, it will definitely have more than enough. Japan has already achieved outstanding achievements in economics and culture, and has achieved the status of an advanced country in East Asia. The people are diligent and hardworking, and they share the characteristics of the Eastern race with the Chinese people. From an economic point of view, what Japan lacks in production is often surplus in China, and what China needs in materials is enough for Japan to supply. In this way, the so-called operation of the economic group is not only the happiness of the East Asian countries and nations, but also the happiness of world peace. Moreover, the current Red Disaster in Northwest China is raging. If this international route, which the Communist Party has long been planning, is opened up, what will East Asia look like at that time? Thinking about it, we should not be chilled. The reason why we believe that East Asian economic cooperation must start from China and Japan is another reason. Conflicts between China and Japan in past political measures have also been caused by poor economic relations. Take a look at the political loans for participating in the war and the production loans for railways, mines, forests, and telecommunications. As for joint ventures in banking, factories, and mines, the total amount is more than 700 million yuan. The former debts could not be repaid, and the latter operations were not profitable. The lending and receiving parties accumulated many evil causes, resulting in the previous evil. Since the proposal of economic cooperation has been initiated by Japan, it is better for China to accept it reluctantly than to take the initiative to expand its cooperation. Acceptance has the nature of coercion, but if we cooperate automatically, we can prepare for consultations in advance and respond well, and the parties can also participate in the plan and express their opinions. Moreover, economic groups inherently have the purpose of common interests. The so-called "rule" and the so-called "scope" are part of the method and depend on harmonious exploration. The only thing that is required is that all East Asian countries, for the sake of leading the alliance, must be absolutely equal, regardless of whether they are China or Japan, to maintain the status of sovereign independence. Second, regardless of whether it is an agricultural country or an industrial country, each should be given the opportunity to develop its abilities without restrictions, in order to conform to the principle of mutual benefit. Third, countries outside of East Asia, although not within the group, should not infringe on their acquired benefits, in order to dispel the misunderstanding of the Asian Monroe Doctrine. Fourth, the cooperative procedure should start with the development of the North China region, which is called the habit, because the area south of the Yangtze River in China has long formed its special economic scope, and the red trend in the northwest border is dangerous. Then gradually spread to various places, in order to achieve realistic possibilities. According to these four points, follow the trend, and by the rule and management, the economic coordination between China and Japan, and then the political solution, will not be difficult. The reason why we believe that Sino-Japanese economic cooperation must first start with the development of North China is another reason. Narrowing down from East Asian economic relations to Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, and further narrowing down from the Sino-Japanese economic group to North China development, seems to imply that the meaning is not broad, and the undertaking is not difficult. In fact, there are thousands of threads, and if the end is not found, there is no way to manage it. Let's talk about the factual aspect. In recent times, the North China region, according to the general habit of interpretation, includes Chahar, Suiyuan, Shanxi, and Shandong as the boundary. However, the mountains, rivers, railways, and shipping routes of these provinces, whether natural or artificial, cannot be forcibly divided from other provinces, so the production benefits are also closely related. For example, Shanxi coal is sold to Shanghai, and Henan needs brine salt. Within the five provinces, transportation, construction, water conservancy, and agricultural products, such as the Cangshi and Baoning railways, are in urgent need of expansion, and the railways and highways of Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, and Suiyuan are in urgent need of connection. The cotton industry in Hebei and Shandong, and the animal husbandry in Chahar and Suiyuan, are in urgent need of improvement. If there is an operation at this time, the design is still pending. The economic situation in North China has been forced by years of floods, droughts, and wars. The rural areas are declining, and industry and commerce are depressed, resulting in reduced production and weakened purchasing power. According to customs reports, the total import and export of the region has declined, and food and population account for a large proportion. It can be said that the whole region is suffering. How can there be surplus power for development? As for technical talent, China has always lacked it. There is a precedent for cooperation with European and American experts. If we focus on the actual issues of industry, agriculture, etc., which are needed in China and Japan, and in North China at the present time, the improvement and facilities are greatly dependent on the guidance and guidance of Japanese specialists. Therefore, from the perspective of both capital and technology, the connection and introduction are indispensable. Secondly, from the theoretical aspect, the political disputes between China and Japan have not been resolved, and the seriousness of the North China issue can be found everywhere. In the past, Sino-Japanese joint ventures have often been stranded halfway or fundamentally dissipated due to the influence of prestige or situation. Now that there is reasonable and well-intentioned economic cooperation, all previous misunderstandings should be swept away. The key lies in the fact that there is a need for factual evidence, and it cannot be done without a long time. Construction projects such as opening mines, building roads, and improving land are all in close contact with the people, and common misunderstandings are unavoidable. It is planned to broadly gather local aspirations and appoint officials to alleviate them. The benefits of joint ventures must be promoted in advance through news and illustrations to avoid dissenting opinions. Therefore, these works are extremely important in cooperation. Colleagues, in view of the above-mentioned facts and theories, have one thing that hinders the development of North China, and the entire East Asian economic relationship cannot be completed. Therefore, we have initiated the East Asia Economic Association, and we are very willing to shoulder this mission and be the pioneers for our countrymen. Moreover, the fact that there has been political deterioration between China and Japan in the past is in no way the responsibility of the people of both sides. Therefore, the national economy of both sides has the freedom to cooperate. Now, one government has explicitly issued a statement of warning to its neighbors, and one government is advocating economic cooperation. Colleagues are humbly taking part in this, and we are ashamed of our meager efforts. However, we are mindful of the dangers and chaos, and it is the responsibility of everyone. Especially in the corner of North China, whether it is related to our hometown or we have been traveling for a long time, we are driven by justice and should fulfill our natural duties. Mencius once told King Xuan of Qi, "Those who delight in Heaven will preserve the world, and those who fear Heaven will preserve their country." He also quoted the words of King Tai of Zhou to tell Duke Wen of Teng, "I have heard that a gentleman does not harm people with what he uses to nourish them." We hope that the people of East Asia will all be in awe of Heaven's Mandate and strive to be gentlemen who nourish people. We will not refrain from speaking out and dare to exhaust our sincerity. We hereby declare!"

The Yanhai River Bursts: The Situation in Banpu is Critical; Important Documents of the Salt Affairs Audit Office Moved into the City; Ships Sealed and Laborers Conscripted to Build Embankments in Case of Emergency 85

Guanyun Correspondence: When the Yellow River enters Jiangsu, Xu Prefecture is the first to bear the brunt. Since the Liutang River breached, Donghai, Guanyun, and Shuyang counties will once again be flooded. At present, in the Guanyun area, because the Chaimi River cannot be protected, they have to retreat to the Jian River. However, the water level is increasing day by day, and the situation is becoming more and more urgent. On the 1st and 2nd of this month, the water level increased exceptionally due to the tide. On the morning of the 3rd, the water level increased even more than on the 1st and 2nd. Because the sea tide was pushing upwards, the river water could not be discharged. After the Liutang Dike broke, the Chaimi River was also difficult to defend. Currently, the Yanhe River embankment is being raised, outside the Dananmen gate in Banpu, all the way to Xin'an Town, and then south to the embankment outside the Ximen gate in Lianshui. All of them are conscripting laborers to build them. People are panicking, as if a great disaster is about to happen. Early on the 4th, the north end of Dayishan Street was flooded, and the water outside the Banpu embankment was also not small. They are currently repairing the embankment and building new embankments, doing their best. The water level on the highway from Banpu to Dayi Xinpu is only one foot high. Many civilian ships have been sealed outside the Dananmen gate in case of emergency. In short, the work of blocking the breach in Shandong cannot be done urgently, and the Qingjiang Canal is not allowing diversion, so it is difficult to be optimistic about Haizhou. Ordinary autumn beans cannot be harvested until after the middle of the ninth lunar month. Wheat should have been sown early, but the farmers are watching the water level and cannot sow quickly. If the sowing of wheat is delayed again, even if the flood does not expand, there will be famine next spring. Currently, grain prices are rising, and firewood is not easy to buy, with supply exceeding demand. The Salt Affairs Audit Office outside the Xiaonanmen gate in Banpu is based there, and the distance from the water surface is limited. It is heard that on the evening of the 3rd, important documents were moved into the embankment. (October 4th)

Bandit Suppression in Various Provinces: Road Network About to be Completed; Over Ten Provinces Including Hubei and Sichuan Have Largely Established Connections; The Executive Headquarters Has Overseen the Completion of Over 20,000 Li of Roads. 86

Hankou Correspondence: Road construction is an important task within the bandit suppression area, its effectiveness comparable to that of blockhouses. Its relationship to culture, politics, economics, and transportation is also profound. After the establishment of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces, great attention was paid to the development of highways. In November of the 21st year (of the Republic), the headquarters convened a highway conference of seven provinces—Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Hunan, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Jiangsu—to plan the trunk and branch lines of highways in the seven provinces. The scope of construction projects was also expanded to include parts of Shaanxi, Gansu, Sichuan, Guizhou, and Hunan provinces. The method of supervision involved submitting each province’s highway engineering plans and budgets to the Executive Headquarters for approval. For highways of significant importance to military transport in the bandit suppression effort, the Executive Headquarters would, if necessary, dispatch personnel to supervise the construction and subsidize the expenses, in addition to requiring the provincial governments to complete the construction within a specified time. Regarding the administrative system for supervision, general highways were handled by the Fifth Division, with the cooperation of the Transportation Division and the First Division. Highways of significant importance to military operations in the bandit suppression effort were handled by the First Division, with the cooperation of the Transportation Division and the Fifth Division. Highways built by military engineers were planned by the Military Engineering Construction Committee and personnel were dispatched to construct them. In addition, the Executive Headquarters also established a Highway Division to specifically oversee the construction of designated highways. The most recent establishment was the Sichuan-Guizhou Provinces Highway Supervision Office, which specializes in supervising the construction and traffic management of highways in those two provinces. Because each entity is responsible for its own duties, things are carried out in an orderly manner. Currently, the total length of completed and under-construction highways in nine provinces—Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Fujian, Shaanxi, Gansu, Guizhou and Fujian—up to the end of the 23rd year (of the Republic) is as follows: (1) Henan: 2,271 kilometers completed, 458 kilometers under construction; (2) Hubei: 192 kilometers completed, 497 kilometers under construction; (3) Anhui: 4,400 kilometers completed, 303 kilometers under construction; (4) Jiangxi: 4,900 kilometers completed, 1,384 kilometers under construction; (5) Fujian: 2,532 kilometers completed, 836 kilometers under construction; (6) Shaanxi: 1,676 kilometers completed, 522 kilometers under construction; (7) Gansu: 1,353 kilometers completed, 158 kilometers under construction; (8) Sichuan: 304 kilometers completed, construction details not yet reported; (9) Guizhou: 1,574 kilometers completed, construction details not yet reported. The total is 20,202 kilometers completed and 3,158 kilometers under construction, with Jiangxi ranking first, followed by Anhui and Henan, and Gansu having the least. Recently completed and under-construction trunk lines of significant importance to military operations in the bandit suppression effort are even more numerous, most of them being inter-provincial highways with relatively long routes, including those connecting Sichuan, Hunan, Guizhou, Xikang, Gansu, Shaanxi, Hubei, Henan, etc. Their names are as follows: (1) Hunan-Guizhou Road: From Changsha to Guiyang, the western Hunan section has been completed and opened to traffic, but the section from Yuanling to Nianyu Pu has not yet been paved. The eastern Guizhou section is being rushed, and is now barely open to traffic. (2) Sichuan-Guizhou Road: From Chengdu to Guiyang, the entire road has been completed and opened to traffic. (3) Sichuan-Hubei Road: From Hankou to Chengdu, the Hankou-Yichang section within Hubei has long been completed and opened to traffic, and the pavement is now being laid. The Yangtze River flood this year has greatly affected the engineering project on this road. The earth road of the Badong section was completed and opened to traffic at the end of September. The Shilipu section has been surveyed and is about to be constructed. The section from Yichang to Badong is more difficult to build because it must pass through the Yangtze River. Currently, the Yangtze River is used for intermodal transport. Within Sichuan Province, the route is 925 kilometers long, of which 520 kilometers have been completed, and the remaining 405 kilometers can be completed soon. (4) Sichuan-Shaanxi Road: From Chengdu to Xi'an, within Sichuan Province, traffic has been opened to Langzhong. The section from Langzhong to the Sichuan provincial border is being supervised by the Highway Supervision Office. Within Shaanxi Province, traffic has been opened to Baoji. The section from Baoji to Hanzhong is under construction. The section from Hanzhong to the Shaanxi provincial border is still in the planning stage. (5) Sichuan-Xikang Road: From Chengdu to Kangding, the Chengdu-Ya'an section and the Kangding-Luding section have been completed and opened to traffic. The Luding-Ya'an section is being rushed. (6) Sichuan-Gansu Road: From Chengdu to Lanzhou, within Sichuan Province, traffic has been opened from Chengdu to Jiangyou. The section from Jiangyou to the Sichuan provincial border is being rushed. Within Gansu Province, traffic has been opened from Lanzhou to Dingxi. The section from Dingxi to Tianshui is under construction. The section from Tianshui to the Gansu provincial border is being surveyed. (7) Hunan-Shaanxi Road: From Hankou to Xi'an, within Hubei Province, traffic has been opened from Hankou to Baihe, but the roadbed of the section from Laohekou to Baihe has been washed away by heavy floods and cannot be used for traffic. Within Shaanxi Province, the section from Hanzhong to Ankang is under construction, and the Ankang to Baihe section has been surveyed and will be built soon. (8) Luoyang-Tongguan Road: From Luoyang to Tongguan, the entire road is under construction. (9) Xi'an-Jingziguan Road: From Xi'an to Jingziguan, the entire road is under construction. (10) Xi'an-Lanzhou Road: From Xi'an to Lanzhou, the entire road has been completed and opened to traffic. (12) Southern Hubei Road: From Wuchang to the southern Hubei border, the entire road was opened to traffic at the end of September. Looking at the highway construction situation in the above provinces, it can be seen that the highway network within the bandit suppression area is about to be completed. (4th)

Cheng Hai Fisherman Nets Submarine Aircraft --Location Outside Shantou Port-- 87

Shantou Correspondence: People in Caocaojiao, Chenghai County, are mostly engaged in the fishing industry. After the autumn winds rise, fishing boats form fleets and operate on the sea. On September 24th, several Heshengfa-branded fishing boats sailed near the Shantou harbor to fish. Several boats towed nets, riding the wind and waves. Before long, the nets gradually became heavy, and then the boats were restrained and could not move. The fishermen were overjoyed, thinking they had caught a large school of golden threadfin bream. Since the net was heavy and could not be lifted, they hurriedly dove to the bottom of the sea to see what it was. They discovered that what the net had caught was a huge aircraft that could carry more than a dozen people, with all kinds of equipment inside. The fishermen initially suspected that it was a submarine aircraft. After the tide receded, several fishermen and workers used large ropes and exerted great effort to hoist the aircraft up. The net was already tattered. First, the wings were removed, but the fuselage was so large that several boats could not load it, so they had to let it sink back into the sea. Several pieces of the wings and steering gear were removed and transported back. However, the fishermen's large net was already broken.

Suzhou: Thugs Commit Robbery with Knives Late at Night 88

At about 10 p.m. on the 4th, Zeng Zihong, a teacher at Chunyi Middle School, and his wife, Ms. Wu, returned home after watching a movie at the Suzhou Grand Theater in the North Bureau. When they passed the entrance of the Bamboo Lane of the Horse Doctor Section, they suddenly encountered a thug who grabbed Ms. Wu, showed a sharp blade to threaten her. Ms. Wu was shocked and screamed, and fled into a nearby clothing store. Her husband, Zeng Zihong, rushed up to resist the thug, who stabbed Zeng's left arm and fled. Zeng shouted loudly for the police, who chased him to Erduo Bin Lane and arrested the thug. He was handed over to the Shan Police District. He confessed his name as Lu Guangting, a local resident living at No. 40, Liujia浜. He was then transferred to the Public Security Bureau on the 5th and then to the local court for handling.

Wuxi: Confiscated Cocoon Boats Case Resolved 89

Our county's Dacheng Silk Factory set up a station near Xushe in Yixing this year to purchase autumn cocoons and dried them into 1,066 bales. These were loaded onto four boats and were about to be transported when they were detained by the residents of the 6th District of the county. The Silk Factory Association of our county telegraphed the provincial government, requesting that the Yixing county government be ordered to dispatch police to escort the confiscated cocoons out of the county. However, they were blocked by hundreds of residents of the district. The former magistrate of Guanxing County, Xiao, then sent Zheng Xin, the captain of the 3rd Security Brigade, to lead more than ten officers to Xushe to protect the cocoon boats. He also worked with Zhou Yuanxun, the model district chief of our county's cocoon community, to mediate with all their strength. The matter has now been completely resolved. The confiscated cocoon boats had already set sail for Wuxi yesterday.

Joint Petition of Department Store and Silk Fabric Businesses 90

The local department store and silk fabric trade associations pointed out that the Shanghai National Goods Promotion Association came to Wuxi this time for temporary auctions and had not heard of paying the taxes due. However, according to the Provisional Constitution, people have the obligation to pay taxes, and equality is required by law. Why should the same merchant have to bear local taxes when doing business here, while out-of-town merchants temporarily avoid them? They were unwilling to accept this, so they elected representatives yesterday to petition the county government, requesting that all local taxes and levies due by various industries be waived or temporarily allowed to be recorded as debt during the association's auction period, in order to reduce costs and show small businesses equal treatment. Shao Jingren, the chief of the First Section, came out to receive them and replied to the representatives that the National Exhibition Hall would also be charged rent for the period of one month. The collection of business taxes would be handled by the business tax collection office. The representatives were not satisfied and left.

The construction materials for the telephone installation in Wujin Township by the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department have already been transported to Changzhou. The Provincial Exchange Office has been ordered to send an acting engineer, Shi Youzheng, to lead workers to Changzhou to carry out the construction within a few days. The planned route and distance for the installation are: from the city to Qishuyan, a total of 12 kilometers; from Shangmei to Biniu, a total of 6 kilometers. Long-distance wooden poles are already in place. Now it is planned to lay new lines. From the city to Qishuyan to Hengshanqiao, a total of 8 kilometers; from Shangmei to Biniu to Xixiashu, a total of 11 kilometers; from the city to Boyiqiao, a total of 6 kilometers; from Xiaxieqiao to Shili Town, a total of 28 kilometers, are all planned to have new wooden poles erected. The project is to be completed and the telephones operational within a specified period.

Bishop Cai Ning inspected church affairs and arrived in Hangzhou on the 1st. After completing his work, he arrived in He on the 4th. All the members of the main churches in Jiaxing also came to the station to greet him. Hangzhou: Salt Farmers from Daishan Come to Hangzhou to Petition 95

Salt farmers from the Daishan salt fields in Dinghai were not compensated for the salt quota set for the five districts under their jurisdiction, causing panic among the livelihoods of more than 10,000 salt farmers. They specially sent representatives Zhou Fengxian, Zhang Tongli and others to Shanghai to negotiate with the salt management, but there were no satisfactory results. The representatives then went from Shanghai to Hangzhou. Yesterday (5th), they went to the Liangzhe Salt Transport Office to petition. The transport envoy, Zhou Zonghua, received them and promised to order the salt merchants to collect the salt at a 60% discount, as per the example of eastern Zhejiang, and ordered the salt merchants to comply immediately. The representatives of the salt farmers reluctantly accepted and immediately returned to Daishan in Dinghai to report. (Important).

The required funding is extremely large and is currently being discussed.

Local News: Chairman Lin Departs Beijing for Shanghai 97

Lin Sen, Chairman of the National Government, departed Beijing at 11 o'clock last night on a special train attached to the Beijing-Shanghai night express train and is heading to Shanghai. He arrived at 7:15 this morning. Tang Youren, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, came with him.

President Sun Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday. He said that the Italy-Abyssinia War Would Not Expand and that he Approves of Mr. Yan’s Land Village System

According to the Central News Agency, Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, left Beijing by night train at 11 p.m. the night before and arrived at Zhenru at 7:10 a.m. yesterday. He went straight to his private residence on Columbia Road to rest. At noon, he met with reporters and made the following remarks:

The Italy-Abyssinia War Will Not Expand

Italy and Abyssinia have already started a war, and the eyes of the world are focused on the war. People are worried that the future development of the war will restart a world war. However, according to my observation, the Italy-Abyssinia war will not expand, because both Britain and France are unwilling to use force to sanction the situation in Europe, so they will not be dragged into the war. A second world war will not break out because of this. In the future, at most, the countries will only make moral sanctions and appeals for justice. As for the war between Italy and Abyssinia, if Abyssinia is defeated and suffers a miserable defeat, a peaceful solution can be expected soon. Otherwise, the war will be prolonged. But in any case, Italy will not be able to achieve its ultimate goal of eliminating Abyssinia and making it a complete colony, because Britain and France are watching from the sidelines. The war between Italy and Abyssinia has little impact on the Far East, but it would be an exception if it caused a world war.

The Land Village System Can be Tried

Yan Xishan, Director of Pacification of Shanxi Province, advocates the land village system and is willing to use Shanxi Province as a pilot area. This proposal has been submitted to Zhao Pilian to send to the National Government as soon as possible. After the Central Political Conference makes a decision, it will be implemented on a trial basis. The Kuomintang originally regarded land nationalization as the highest and ultimate goal for people's livelihood issues. Before land nationalization is implemented, the emergence of large landlords will be restricted, and the system of farmers owning the land they cultivate will be implemented first. Now, Mr. Yan resolutely advocates the land village system and has the courage to use Shanxi Province as a pilot area, which is admirable.

Southwest Central Committee Members Attend the Plenary Session

The Southwest Central Committee members have decided to attend the Sixth Plenary Session. It was reported that Hu Zhan Tang, Guang Sheng, had left Europe for the United States. Mr. Hu may stay in the United States for a long time and then return to China. The Legislative Yuan will hold a meeting next week, which happens to be National Day, so it has been decided to convene it one day earlier.

Nine Major Groups, Including the City Chamber of Commerce, Hosted a Banquet for Sir Otto Niemeyer Last Night; Guo Bingwen Delivered a Welcome Speech on Behalf of the Groups, Hoping for Accurate Reporting of the Chinese Situation. 98

Nine major groups, including the City Chamber of Commerce, the Local Association, the Bankers' Association, the Money Dealers' Association, the China General Chamber of Industry, the International Trade Association, the Pacific International Society, the Chinese Students' Global Association, and the International Problems Research Association, held a grand public banquet at the Bankers' Club on the fifth floor of the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road at 8 o'clock last night to welcome Sir Otto Niemeyer, a British economic expert. Chinese cuisine was served, divided into four tables. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until 10 o'clock before the banquet ended. The details are as follows:

Guests and Hosts at the Banquet

The guests and hosts included Sir Otto Niemeyer and his entourage, Ba Zhi and Rogers, as well as the British Consul-General in Shanghai, Bailinan, and representatives from various groups: Yu Zuoting, Chen Zhetan, Ge Jiechen, Du Yuesheng, Hu Yunqiu, Feng Binglu, Chen Guangfu, Yuan Songsun, Zhu Ziliang, Qin Runqing, Xi Jiming, Pei Yunqing, Wang Qiyu, Cai Shengbai, Qian Chengxu, Zhang Yuqiu, Lin Kanghou, Zou Bingwen, Luo Chuanhua, Liu Yuwan, Zhu Youyu, Zhu Shaoping, Li Denghui, Zhou Fanping, Xu Xinliu, Chen Liting, Cao Yunxiang, Liu Hongsheng, Liu Hongen, Li Zhaohuan, Zhang Gongquan, He Dekui, Dong Xian Guang, Tu Chuyu, Rong Qin Kun, and others, totaling more than 30 people.

Mr. Guo’s Speech

After the chairman, Chen Zheqing, took his seat, Mr. Guo Bingwen delivered a welcome speech in English on behalf of the associations, the gist of which was as follows: "Our associations are holding this public banquet here tonight for Sir Otto Niemeyer. We are deeply honored by Sir's presence. Sir is a famous British financial expert who was dispatched to China this time to investigate the economic situation. Some of the rumors in the past about Sir's mission to China have been denied by Sir himself, and some have not been expressed by Sir. However, we firmly believe that with Sir's perseverance, this trip will definitely have good results, making the relationship between China and Britain closer. We believe that Sir will be able to report the real situation in China to the British government and hope to make correct suggestions to the British government. We would like to offer a toast to Sir's good health and happiness."

Sir Otto Niemeyer's Reply: Sir Otto Niemeyer's reply can be roughly divided into three points: 1. Because I have been in China for a short time, I am not yet clear about the Chinese situation, so I cannot make any contributions for the time being. However, I feel that what China needs most at the moment is peace, stability, and commerce. If the government can show more ability in governance, its recovery of strength can be expected. 2. It is rumored that I came here with a large amount of funds, which is an inaccurate guess, because the situations of the Chinese and British governments are very different. In China, the government often invests in the development of industries, while in Britain, it is mostly done by private individuals. 3. It is also rumored that I came here with an economic invasion, which is also a misunderstanding. China's prosperity is not only beneficial to Britain but also has a great relationship with the prosperity of the world. The relationship between China and Britain is on an equal footing.
