Three Types of Government Bonds Redeemed by Lottery This Morning; 23 Lots Drawn, with Redemption Totaling 2.16 Million; Financial and Silk Industry Redemption on the 15th, Disbandment Redemption at the End of the Month 100

The 25th redemption lottery for the Short-Term Financial Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20, the 7th redemption lottery for the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20, and the 21st redemption lottery for the Disbandment Bonds of the Republic of China Year 18 were held at the Bankers' Association at 10 a.m. this morning. More than 30 representatives from all walks of life attended. Jiang Lufu, the director of the Public Debt Department, presided over the lottery of 23 lots with a redemption total of 2.16 million. The redemption of the Financial Short-Term and Jiangzhe Silk Industry bonds will begin on the 15th of this month, and the redemption of the Disbandment Bonds will begin on the 21st of this month, handled by the Central, China, Communications, and other banks. The details are as follows:

Chairman's Report

After the formalities were completed, Chairman Jiang Lufu reported, saying in summary: "Today is the 15th redemption of the Short-Term Financial Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20, the 7th redemption of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20, and the 21st redemption of the Disbandment Bonds of the Republic of China Year 18. We are honored to have you all attend. The total amount of the Short-Term Financial Bonds of Year 20 is 80 million yuan. Apart from the first to fourteenth redemptions, this is the fifteenth redemption, with 17 lots drawn, each lot worth 80,000 yuan, for a total of 1.36 million yuan, which is one-thousandth of the total issued amount of the bonds. Therefore, the method of drawing lots is to use the same three digits at the end of the number as the winning bond. The actual issued amount of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Bonds of Year 20 is 6 million yuan. Apart from the first to sixth redemptions, this is the seventh redemption, with five lots drawn, each lot worth 60,000 yuan, for a total of 300,000 yuan, which is 5% of the total issued amount of the bonds. Therefore, the method of drawing lots is to use the same two digits at the end of the number as the winning bond. In addition, the total amount of the Disbandment Bonds of Year 18 is 50 million yuan. Apart from the first to twentieth redemptions, this is the twenty-first redemption, with one lot drawn, worth 500,000 yuan, which is 1% of the total issued amount of the bonds. Therefore, the method of drawing lots is also to use the same two digits at the end of the number as the winning bond. The above three types of winning bonds, the Short-Term Financial Bonds of Year 20 and the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Bonds of Year 20, will be redeemed starting on the 15th of this month, and the Disbandment Bonds of Year 18 will be redeemed starting on the 21st of this month. Apart from the Silk Industry Bonds, which will be redeemed by the Central, China, Communications, and National Goods banks, the rest will still be handled by the Central, China, and Communications banks, along with the accrued interest, and will be paid in national currency, regardless of location. Please ask the supervisors to check the lots and the ledger for drawing lots for the execution of the lottery."

Winning Numbers

After the chairman finished his report, the supervisors checked the lots and the ledger for drawing lots, and then executed the lottery. The winning numbers are as follows: (1) 17 lots of the Short-Term Financial Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20: No. 078, No. 158, No. 196, No. 203, No. 353, No. 229, No. 471, No. 433, No. 549, No. 671, No. 618, No. 770, No. 704, No. 80, No. 819, No. 951, No. 911. (2) 5 lots of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry Bonds of the Republic of China Year 20: No. 06, No. 36, No. 48, No. 62, No. 79. (3) One lot of the Disbandment Bonds of Year 18: No. 01. The total amount of these bonds to be redeemed is 1.16 million yuan. The lottery ended and the meeting adjourned at 11 o'clock.

Hong Kong National Bank's Shanghai Branch; Creditors Urge Liquidation; Submit Request to Ministry of Finance 101

A Central News Agency report states that since the Hong Kong National Bank suspended operations some time ago, no concrete solution has been announced. The creditors of the Shanghai branch, concerned about their deposits, have formed a creditors' group to pursue recovery. Recently, in addition to the group and its legal counsel, Lawyer Liang Yaobing, sending letters to Lu Zhongqing and Huang Jiyan, former managers of the Shanghai branch, they also submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, urging them to take charge. The text of their petition is excerpted below:

Petition to the Ministry of Finance for Liquidation

The creditors' group submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "The Shanghai branch of the Hong Kong National Bank has been closed for quite some time. Although reports indicate that the bank convened a meeting of its head office creditors and shareholders in Hong Kong on the 28th of last month, the results remain shrouded in secrecy. The creditors' deposits amount to a considerable sum, and they cannot afford to abandon them indefinitely. Furthermore, the end of the year is approaching, and financial difficulties are becoming acute. We respectfully implore your Ministry, which is in charge of national finance, to oversee all banking matters. Now that the creditors have nowhere else to turn, they are compelled to request your esteemed leadership to uphold justice, so that the savings of orphans, widows, and those relying on them for sustenance and funeral expenses may not be squandered in vain. We humbly submit the following liquidation measures: (1) Please promptly order the bank to submit its assets to the Ministry for liquidation. (2) Please appoint impartial personnel from among the responsible individuals of the Bankers' Association to oversee the liquidation process. (3) If the bank is unwilling to surrender its assets, please order all debtors of the bank not to return their debts to the National Bank but to the Bankers' Association, so that the personnel appointed by the Bankers' Association may proceed with liquidation. Respectfully submitted to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance."

Creditors' Remarks

Furthermore, a responsible person from the association told reporters that the collapse of the Hong Kong National Bank was undoubtedly an unfortunate event. Recent news of its potential reopening has been welcomed by all creditors. However, this news of reopening has only appeared in the newspapers, and the bank's representatives have not provided any clear confirmation. This is no different from an unsigned check. Therefore, the creditors dare not trust it. Moreover, once a bank has collapsed, even if it reopens, its credibility will plummet. Rumors of converting deposits into shares are unacceptable to the creditors. The group will fight to the death to protect their interests. It has also been found that some Chinese merchants, using foreign names, are unwilling to hand over their assets to Chinese government agencies for public liquidation after the collapse. This not only harms the interests of creditors but also sets a dangerous precedent. Therefore, we hope that the Ministry of Finance will use extraordinary measures, decisively and swiftly, to break this bad habit. We also hope that compatriots across the country will rise up to support us.

Trustcor Bank Suspends Operations; Appoints Accountant Huang Peiqi for Liquidation 105

Trustcor Bank, Shanghai Main Branch and Harbin and Hulun branches, Xiahfei Road branch, after a board meeting, simultaneously announced their suspension of operations yesterday morning, entrusting Accountant Huang Peiqi with liquidation. The liquidation office is located at 149 Sichuan Road. Details are as follows:

Bank History

Trustcor Bank of America was founded by Mr. S. Kriger, the former manager of the Harbin Yong Sheng Company. It was established in 1927 in accordance with the laws of Nevada, USA, with its head office in Harbin. In 1928, a branch was established in Hulun. In 1929, a branch was established in Shanghai. In 1934, to facilitate business development, the head office was relocated to 100 Jiujiang Road, Shanghai, Harbin branch became Shanghai branch, and a branch was set up at 774 Xiahfei Road, intersection of Jin Shenfu Road. It has correspondent banks in various countries around the world, with a paid-up capital of US$100,000. Its main business includes general deposits, remittances, and trust services. Its reserve fund amounts to US$27,750.

Resolution to Suspend Operations

Chairman and Manager Kriger and Manager Makoroff, E. K. Makoroff, due to the impact of the Northeast Incident, found it impossible to maintain operations. A board meeting at 11:00 PM on October 4 decided to cease operations. Starting yesterday morning, the head office on Jiujiang Road, the branch on Xiahfei Road, and the branches in Harbin and Hulun were all ordered by the board of directors to suspend operations. At the same time, an English notice of suspension of liquidation was posted, which translates as "The bank, pursuant to a resolution passed by the Board of Directors at 11:00 PM on October 4, 1935, has suspended operations pending the selection of a liquidator."

Notice of Liquidation

Accountant Huang Peiqi, representing Trustcor Bank, announced yesterday, "According to a statement from representatives of Trustcor Bank, the bank has been operating smoothly since its establishment. However, the Harbin branch has been unable to sustain operations due to the impact of the incident and suspended operations. The bank is unable to support itself independently and has decided to liquidate. We should announce on its behalf that all creditors are requested to present their claims for registration within fourteen days for verification. Debtors are also expected to return their debts within the same period. Otherwise, we will take legal action. This is hereby announced, and the liquidation office is located at 149 Sichuan Road, 4th Floor."

Reasons for Suspension

A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency visited Lawyer Chen Daxun, the legal counsel to the bank, yesterday. According to him, Trustcor Bank was established in the sixth year of the Republic of China and was originally registered in the United States, with branches on Xiahfei Road and in Harbin. The business has been stable, with a capital of US$100,000. Most of the customers are overseas Chinese and Russians. However, the global economic downturn has had an impact. Since the September 18th Incident, the Harbin branch has been greatly affected, and the bank's situation has become difficult. Deposit withdrawals have reached 70 percent. However, the bank has been able to cope. However, after the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, over 25,000 Russian employees returned to their country, further impacting the bank's operations. Therefore, it was decided to liquidate. It is also said that, according to a report from the parties involved, the bank has deposits of 280,000, but assets of over 300,000. After offsetting all income and expenses, a liquidator has been appointed and a solution should be found soon, so that depositors will not suffer losses.

According to the Great American Evening Post, Trustcor Bank, located in Shanghai, is run by Russians with head office in Shanghai and branches in Harbin and Hailar. It has suspended operations today (5th). Under supervision of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, it is now under liquidation. A notice written in English was posted on the door of the Bank located at No.100 Jiujiang Road which says “the Bank ceases operations in accordance with the resolution passed by the Board of Directors on the 4th of October, 1935, to await the appointment of a liquidator”. In front of the Xiahfei Road branch, No. 714, there were many people gathering in the morning, most of them Russians. The Head Office, however, was rather quiet. Most of the depositors were Russians, therefore the suspension of the bank did not affect the financial market of Shanghai. According to Law Office of Luo, the bank’s staff members guaranteed that the assets of Shanghai Bank exceed the deposits amount by a large margin. Liquidation will be done soon and the deposits are expected to be fully returned in a short period of time. The Bank suspended operation mainly because, after the Chinese Eastern Railway was sold to Japan, around 25,000 Russian people left Harbin. This caused the Harbin branch to be in a difficult situation. Due to the economic depression in Shanghai, 70 percent of the Shanghai Branch's deposits were withdrawn in the past four months. This was a fatal strike. The Bank was run by Russians. Almost all of its staff members were Russians. However, it obtained the license of Nevada. That is why “America” was added to the name of the Bank. However, it was not registered at the American Consulate General in Shanghai or Harbin. The liquidation was not submitted for approval to the American Court in China. It would be rejected if it were submitted now, since this bank is not an American merchant’s firm and is not related to American interest. The American authorities in Shanghai will not act on the liquidation. The Bank was established in Harbin in 1927 by former staff members of the Sino-Russian Daosheng Bank. As it observed the decline of businesses in Manchuria under Japanese rule, it moved its head office to Shanghai in 1932. According to its Business Notice of November 30th, 1934, its assets and liabilities were 6,867,545 yuan. The ready cash that was available was 44,500 yuan. The capital was 286,740 yuan. The profit and loss of the year was 274,682 yuan.

Chinese Cotton Mills in Difficulties; Requesting Reassessment of Property Rental

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "To the esteemed Council: We have received a letter from the Chinese Cotton Mill Association, stating that Shenxin Textile Mill No. 9, located at 140 Macau Road, pays a quarterly police rate of $5,950. Due to business difficulties, only half of the second floor is in use. Ke Ganchen Urges Expediting the Implementation of Bank Acceptance Drafts; Using Factory Goods as Collateral; To Be Handled by a Committee Formed by the Chamber of Commerce 106

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Committee for Industrial and Commercial Recovery, after resolving to request methods for three issues of increasing chips, has now been promoting them in various quarters. Ke Ganchen, a leader in the cotton cloth industry and currently a standing committee member of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, sent a letter to Wang Yansong, Director of the Recovery Committee, advocating for the urgent promotion of bank acceptance drafts to rescue the stagnation of industry and commerce, and proposing implementation methods. The original letter is recorded below: "In recent years, our country has been shaken externally by the global economic recession, and internally by frequent natural disasters and banditry. Rural areas are bankrupt, and industry and commerce are withering. Domestic funds are concentrated in cities, causing anemia and congestion, which has long become a pathological condition. Since the United States implemented the nationalization of silver last autumn, the price of silver overseas has gradually risen, and a huge amount of our country's silver reserves has flowed out. Those with knowledge are increasingly alarmed by the reduction of silver reserves and the lack of chips to cope. Public opinion is divided, and everyone is thinking of ways to remedy the situation. To this day, there is still no concrete solution. The market is in panic, fearing the imminent arrival of a paper money policy, leading to the flight of capital and market chaos. Without sowing good causes, how can one expect good results? It is indeed regrettable. Now, the Association has boldly put forward the idea of increasing chips, designing comprehensively and elaborating in detail, so that the general public knows that the current lack of chips is a lack of credit chips, not a lack of payment chips. It also clarifies that the remedy lies in transforming stagnation into circulation. Recognizing that industrial securities and bills are credit chips in the modern financial market, it proposes to replace the current factory mortgage with acceptance of corporate bonds, to replace the current movable property mortgage with bank acceptance drafts, and to replace the current credit loans with commercial acceptance drafts, thereby establishing a modern credit system and promoting modern credit chips. This is visionary, insightful, and addresses the current problems. However, although the above three are all ways to transform the financial industry's investment methods, their implementation may differ in difficulty, urgency, and order. Therefore, I offer my humble opinion for your consideration: (1) Although the organization of a guarantee company is governed by special laws enacted by the government and must be registered with and supervised by the competent authorities, it is feared that not many can truly disclose their internal situation. Therefore, if we hope that its own stocks or issued bonds will circulate in the market, there will be the following two difficulties: A. The funds of our country's companies mostly range from tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands at most. The amount is small, and circulation is difficult. Whether it is possible to issue bonds is even more problematic. B. If we want to issue corporate bonds, we must not only clearly calculate the assets and liabilities of the company itself to understand the actual value of its factory property, but also reassure the subscribers. Whether our country's existing corporate organizations can be so sound is still questionable. Therefore, to replace the current factory mortgage with the acceptance of corporate bonds, it is necessary to conduct accurate investigations, detailed statistics, and improve the organization of the company before it is possible. This cannot be achieved overnight and should be carried out by the Association and related organizations with careful planning over time. (2) Replacing credit loans with commercial acceptance drafts is relatively safer. However, because the discounting banks do not have access to rediscounting, they are hesitant to accept as many bills. Moreover, given the decline in modern industrial and commercial credit, they are even more hesitant to wait and see. Therefore, even if they try their best to promote it, they still cannot promote it to its full potential. It can be seen that we must wait directly for the national banks to quickly establish a rediscounting system, and fundamentally establish the economic credit of industry and commerce. (3) The most painful problem for industry and commerce now is the difficulty in turning over goods and the lack of acceptance of mortgages. Because the company's capital has mostly been consumed on real estate, machinery, and productive assets, and in recent years, most of them have overused the assets, there is naturally insufficient liquid capital for business operations. In addition to borrowing from banks and money shops, they mostly rely on goods as chips to mortgage for cash. Since the financial turmoil last year, credit loans have been out of the question. Even goods that were previously used as chips are now being rejected for cash loans from banks and money shops, regardless of the discount. Goods are difficult to sell for the time being, resulting in closure due to lack of turnover. In essence, there are no losses. This situation is most regrettable. The reason why banks and money shops refuse to accept goods for mortgage is nothing more than two reasons: A. They are unable to protect themselves and are afraid that no one will accept the re-pledge, so they have to keep cash on hand to prepare for emergencies. B. They are afraid that the market price will fall too quickly, and the mortgaged goods will be difficult to sell for cash if they are not redeemed by the due date. Or, they are worried that the mortgaged goods are not reliable and that the estimated value is not accurate. If bank acceptance drafts are promoted, the goods will be stored in the bank's godown and completely possessed by the bank. The chips used are fixed-term bills. There is no need to prepare cash before the due date. If there are concerns about the reliability of the mortgaged goods, the accuracy of the valuation, and the appropriateness of the discount, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce can dispatch leaders from various industries to form a committee to provide consultation to banks and money shops and assist them in handling all matters. Since the difficulties encountered by mortgaged goods are eliminated, the banks and money shops will naturally be happy to promote them. The central bank's rediscounting will also have no concerns. Therefore, among the three options in the original opinion letter, option B is the easiest to implement and is also what industry and commerce most eagerly hope for. To transform stagnation into circulation, there is no better plan than this. I dare to ask that we address the most urgent needs first, conduct research, and promote them thoroughly. The banks, money shops, industry, and commerce will all benefit. What could be more fortunate?

Municipal Police Bureau Expediting Filling of Opium Addict Licenses 107

According to a Central News Agency report, since the Municipal Police Bureau began registering opium addicts, the registration has been extremely enthusiastic, as reported previously. However, it has been found that all opium addicts who had previously voluntarily applied to the bureau for registration or who had been investigated and advised to register had not yet been issued addiction licenses and were instead issued temporary receipts. To expedite the filling of limited-term rehabilitation licenses for opium addicts to facilitate their receipt of the licenses, starting this month, Dai Lizhen, the section chief of the Opium Addict Registration Section, will supervise the clerks to expedite the filling of licenses day and night, even on weekly holidays. It is said that a batch of rehabilitation licenses has already been completed and will be distributed to various branch offices and stations in the coming days for distribution to the opium addicts under their jurisdiction.

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Municipal Police Bureau has extended the opium addict registration period in the city by one month, and more than 8,000 people have now registered. However, it is feared that some citizens do not fully understand the meaning of opium addict registration, so they are still hesitant to register voluntarily. Amidst the city's strict prohibition of opium, the advisory registration period will end at the end of this month, and compulsory registration will be implemented next month. The tolerance period is only temporary. It seems that it is necessary to make the general public thoroughly understand the meaning of registration. Therefore, they are rushing to produce dozens of opium addict registration Q&A, using simple language in a Q&A format to explain and elaborate on the purpose of the city's opium addict registration, so as to achieve a propaganda effect. Once compiled, they will be distributed to citizens throughout the city.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: Explanation that Invoices Should Be Stamped, Using Letter Format Does Not Exempt It 116

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to Liangxin Weaving Factory yesterday, explaining that invoices in the form of letters should still be stamped. The letter stated: "We received your letter of the 4th of this month, along with two sample invoices. We have examined the provisions of Article 16, Paragraph 3 of the Stamp Tax Law, which states that invoices are required for other industrial and commercial entities listing payments due to customers, which are used as a basis for payment. Article 5 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Stamp Tax Law also has specific provisions. All items traditionally or annually listed with the name, quantity, and value of goods given to customers as the basis for payment are considered invoices and should be stamped according to item 3 of the tax rate table. The sample invoice attached to your letter lists the quantity and amount of goods purchased on a certain day of a certain month. Although it is in the form of a letter, it is essentially an invoice and should be stamped according to law."

Report from the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association: 5% of Chinese People Have Tuberculosis; Medical Expenses Reach 32 Million Per Year; Spitting Everywhere is Like Setting Up a Machine Gun at an Intersection 118

The China Anti-Tuberculosis Association held a members' gathering at the YMCA on Sichuan Road at 3:00 PM yesterday, reporting on the association's work over the past year and discussing future activities. The details are recorded below:

Attendees

These included Lu Bohong, Chairman of the Association; Li Tingan, Vice Chairman; Tong Xingmen, Secretary-General; Fang Kan, physician from the Red Cross Hospital; Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University; and over 300 members and guests. Lu Bohong, Li Tingan, and Tong Xingmen were elected as chairmen to preside over the meeting. Chairman Lu Bohong gave a report.

Chairman's Report

He briefly stated that the Association was founded on the proposal of Mayor Wu and has been in existence for over a year. With the support of various parties and the efforts of the members, although there have been no remarkable achievements, a spirit of continuous effort can be seen everywhere. However, he himself is very busy and will need the assistance of Mr. Li Tingan and all the members in the future. The biggest goal of the Association's future work is to establish a tuberculosis hospital. A site of 100 mu has already been found. He hopes that charitable individuals will provide more assistance to complete this task. Li Tingan then gave a speech, and Tong Xingmen reported on the association's work. The People's Singing Society and Qinghua Middle School sang anti-tuberculosis songs and songs urging people not to spit.

Liu's Speech

Liu Zhanen gave a speech, stating that he recently saw in foreign magazines the proportion of tuberculosis patients in Europe, America, and Japan. In Europe, there are 107 people per 10,000; in America, there are 68 people per 10,000; and in Japan, there are 106 people per 10,000. According to recent statistics, there are 500 people per 10,000 in China. Therefore, the incidence of tuberculosis in China is higher than in any other country in the world. Most of those who die from tuberculosis are middle-aged people between the ages of 20 and 40, who are the backbone of the country. According to recent statistics from the Anti-Tuberculosis Association, the money lost due to treating tuberculosis averages 32 million yuan per year. Therefore, whether in terms of human loss or financial loss, tuberculosis is a great scourge in China. Therefore, we must all rise up to prevent it.

Dr. Fang Discusses the Process of Examining Tuberculosis Sputum. He briefly stated that the association was commissioned by the Anti-Tuberculosis Association to examine the sputum spat by pedestrians on the road. A total of 120 sputum samples were collected from ten roads, including Yuyuan Road, Haig Road, and Jing'an Temple Road. After examination, 10% of them contained tuberculosis bacteria, averaging one sample per road. The danger is as great as setting up a machine gun on every road.

Ding Xijun Invents a Calendar Clock; It Can Automatically Indicate Large Months, Small Months, Leap Months, Etc., Accurately 119

Mr. Ding Xijun has recently invented a calendar clock after 12 years of painstaking research. After repeated tests, the results are amazing. He has made a model of the calendar clock for people to see. In addition to telling the time, it can automatically and accurately indicate large months, small months, regular months, leap months, the seven luminaries, the twelve branches of the day and night, etc., without human intervention, and will remain accurate for many years. All existing calendars will be obsolete from now on, and the calculation of time, weeks, months, and years will be much easier. The clock has a simple and ingenious structure and beautiful decoration. The explanation of its function is as follows: "Month Recording": The lunar calendar circles the earth monthly. It has excess and shortcomings and cannot correspond to the 24 solar terms. The national calendar divides the earth's orbit around the sun into twelve parts, which roughly corresponds to the 24 solar terms, but the earth actually orbits the sun for 365 and a quarter days, and one day accumulates every four years, so a "February 29th" is added every leap year to correspond to it. This calendar clock can naturally switch and report the large month, the average February, and even the leap day every four years, without error and without human assistance. Day Recording: The Earth's rotation in front of the sun is equal to one day and one night. After running for twenty-four hours, this calendar clock will naturally change the date, whether it's a big month or a small month at the end of the month due to different gear structures. The calendar will naturally agree, "Week Recording": Since the custom of one rest day every seven days spread, East Asia called it one week. The seven celestial bodies are combined, namely the Sun, Moon, Fire, Water, Wood, Metal, and Earth. A week is seven days, commonly referred to as Monday, Tuesday, etc. This calendar clock can indicate what day of the week it is every day, and which day of the week, clear and understandable. Time Recording: The Earth's meridian rotation around the sun is one day, which can also be said that the sun surrounds the earth, which is the principle of a boat sailing on the shore. Anciently, one day was divided into twelve hours, and now it is divided into twenty-four hours. In addition to reporting 24 hours, this calendar clock has a solar sphere indicating the twelve branches for practical use. The rest, the minute hand and the fixed moment are generally the same as ordinary clocks and will not be described separately.

Fire on Guangzhao Road, Zhabei; Over 100 Houses Destroyed 121

Recently, due to the dry weather, fires have been frequent, especially in Zhabei. Most of the buildings burned are thatched cottages of the poor. Rice straw is flammable, and the thatched cottages are close together. Therefore, every fire is difficult to extinguish. This has been seen repeatedly in the winter months. At around 5:00 AM yesterday morning, a fire broke out again in the slum area next to the Yilong Cotton Mill, opposite the Guangdong Guild Hall on Guangzhao Road, Zhabei. The fire started at the home of Yin Chunliu, a peddler from Funing, who was careless while cooking breakfast and left the fire unattended in the rice straw. The fire quickly spread to the surrounding houses. The residents woke up from their dreams in panic and fled in haste. Some carried boxes and suitcases, while others helped the elderly and carried the young. The cries and shouts were overwhelming, and the order was disrupted. At this time, the fire intensified and spread to brick houses and buildings. The flames shot into the sky, turning the sky red. The Haifeng Road Police Station nearby heard the alarm and immediately notified the Zhabei fire brigades in various sections. Fire engines rushed to the scene to put out the fire. All the firefighters were brave and eager, and they sprayed water from all directions. The fire was gradually extinguished at around 6:00 AM. As a result, 32 thatched cottages and 29 brick houses were destroyed, totaling over 120 households. The loss was enormous. Yin Chunliu, who started the fire, was taken to the police station for questioning and temporarily detained for further investigation. However, the victims, having lost their homes, became homeless. They sat on the ground near the scene of the disaster, looking emaciated and miserable.

Investigation and Punishment

For the sake of caution, the Bureau of Weights and Measures has specially extended the deadline for a few days, starting next week, so that rice stores that have been omitted can request a re-inspection. Those present included Mao Xiaxuan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Rao Qiangsheng, representative of the Bureau of Social Affairs; and attending committee members Zhao Jinqing, Yan Jiachi, Cheng Dingyi, Xu Yitang, Yan Fuchu, Qiao Nianchun, Yuan Xilian (representing Yang Mingsan), Pan Shiqing, Wang Liangqing, Xu Zhongming, and Xu Zhishou, totaling fifteen people. Xu Zhongming was publicly elected as chairman, and the ceremony was conducted according to protocol. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, followed by the supervisors and directors holding a swearing-in ceremony. Representatives from party and government agencies attended to supervise the oath-taking. Xu Zhongming, Yan Fuchu, and Gu Wenjun were mutually elected as standing committee members, and duties were immediately assigned and matters discussed: (1) Pan Shiqing was appointed as Director of General Affairs, Xu Zhongming as Director of Investigation, Xu Zhishou as Director of Documentation, and Yan Fuchu as Director of Accounting. (2) Regarding how to proceed with soliciting members, it was resolved that committee members would be the natural captains of the solicitation teams, with a one-month deadline for team solicitation. (3) Regarding the establishment of detailed rules of procedure for the association to be followed, it was resolved that committee member Xu Zhongming would draft them and submit them for approval at the next meeting. (4) Regarding the safekeeping of funds, it was decided to appoint responsible personnel. It was resolved to appoint Yan Fuchu as the "economic safekeeping committee member." The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

A Scene of Urban Crime: Deceiving a Woman, Selling Her as a Prostitute, and Then Stealing Her Money Through a Sleight of Hand. Mrs. Wang Jiang Lost Both Her Daughter and Her Money, Crying Bitterly. The Two Criminals Were Finally Arrested, and the Court Should Severely Punish Them. 133

Mrs. Wang Jiang, a Ningbo woman residing on Xiaoshadu Road, has a daughter named A Bao, seventeen years old, who used to work in a yarn factory. The daughter is beautiful and frivolous, and has had an ambiguous relationship with a male colleague. Although Mrs. Wang had heard about it, she could not control her. Recently, she was laid off from the factory and was unemployed at home. Mother and daughter found it difficult to maintain their livelihood. On the 28th of last month, a fellow villager named Bai Yisheng visited her house for a chat and, after learning about the situation, took the opportunity to take Mrs. Wang and A Bao to the Hua'an Hotel on Hankou Road to stay temporarily. He colluded with the fugitive Wei Niuzi to sell A Bao to Wu Asi, a Jiangbei native at 1056 Beijiangxi Road, as a prostitute. Zeng Laofu, from Danyang, joined in as an impartial witness. The price was 175 silver dollars, but the contract stated a loan of 400 dollars. Mrs. Wang received 150 dollars, with the remaining amount being fees for those who wrote the contract. Seeing that Mrs. Wang was foolish and gullible, they immediately handed over 150 silver dollars in banknotes for A Bao's body. Bai Yisheng wrapped them in paper, hired a rickshaw, and told Mrs. Wang to sit on it, telling her to be careful and return home quickly. He then handed over the paper package. Mrs. Wang was very satisfied, put it in her pocket, and went home. When she opened it, the contents of the package had disappeared. She realized that Bai and the others had used a sleight of hand to steal the money. The brothel on Beijiangxi Road also did not recognize her. Having lost both her daughter and her money, she could only cry bitterly. At about 3 PM the day before yesterday, Mrs. Wang passed by Bazhi Road and got into a dispute with Wu Asi and Zeng Laofu. Fang Fucheng, a Cantonese detective, investigated and, after learning the details, arrested them and took them to the Hongkou Police Station for detention. He then went to Wu's house on Beijiangxi Road, retrieved the girl Wang A Bao, and handed her back to her mother. Yesterday morning, Wu and Zeng were sent to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, detailed the events and requested a postponement. Detective Fang then reported on the arrest of the two defendants, presenting the contract for the sale of Wang's daughter. Mrs. Wang and her daughter A Bao also clarified everything. Wu Asi and Zeng Laofu stammered in their confessions. Judge Xiao Xieffen ordered them to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing.

Invention by the China Educational Equipment Factory: Month, Day, Week, Hour Clock. Announcing the Hour, the Time of Day, the Date, the Weekday, and the Month. The Ministry of Industry Granted a Patent and Issued an Award License. The Ministry of Finance Approved an Additional Reward and Exempted it from Transit Tax. 134

The China Educational Equipment Manufacturing Factory, established by the China Bookstore on Kunming Road, Shanghai, manufactures physical and chemical instruments, specimens, and models, selling them at low prices to enrich the experimental equipment of schools and factories. It has been praised by both the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry. Now, it has newly invented a "Month, Day, Week, Hour Clock." Its components are completely self-made, and even the smallest nail or copper sheet is not imported. Foreign countries do not yet have this invention. In addition to reporting the hours, the clock can automatically report the time of day, the date, the day of the week, and the month. Therefore, after purchasing this clock, one can know the current month, day, day of the week, and time of day at a glance. The outer appearance of the clock is generally similar to that of an ordinary clock (see picture). Its distinguishing feature is that the numbers on the clock face have two circles, inner and outer, indicating the hours from 1 to 24. At the bottom of the clock face is a time-of-day face, marking the twelve time periods of Zi, Chou, Yin, Mao, etc. It rotates once every twenty-four hours, turning one time period every two hours. Each time period is further divided into early, middle, and late. In the middle of the clock face is a semi-circle with red and blue circular faces representing the sun and the moon, and their appearance and disappearance can indicate the approximate time of day. At the bottom of the clock are mechanisms for reporting the month, date, and day of the week, with three cloth strips separately marking the date, day of the week, and month. The date cloth strip is in the center, moving once every midnight, and returning to the first day of the month at the end of the month. The weekday cloth strip is on the left, also moving once every midnight, and returning to Sunday after Saturday has passed. The month cloth strip is on the right, moving once at the end of each month, and returning to the first month of the year at the end of the year. All of these are automatically converted without error. The clock is divided into nine categories, each with large, medium, and small sizes. Currently, the medium-sized, second model is being produced in large quantities and sold at a special price. The list price is 160 yuan per clock, and the special price is 96 yuan. It is guaranteed for five years and repaired free of charge. An application for a patent has been submitted to the Ministry of Industry and approved. The Ministry of Finance has specially approved exemption from transit tax and stated in its approval, "The Month, Day, Week, Hour Clock manufactured by the factory has been investigated and reported to have an exquisite design and a wide range of uses. There is little such manufacturing in the country, and it is worthy of encouragement." Its value is evident. Those interested in viewing the clock are welcome to visit the China Bookstore's headquarters or local branches for clarification. If you wish to inspect whether the clock is a domestic invention and self-made, the factory welcomes visits from all circles at any time. Please contact the public relations department of the China Bookstore headquarters.

Shanghai South Tobacco Exchange: Notice to Members to Beware of Counterfeit Cigarettes 135

The Shanghai South Office of the Municipal Tobacco Exchange Association has received repeated reports from members in recent days that someone has been falsely using the name of a Yuntaihe Tobacco Company runner to collect empty "Little Fairy" cigarette packs from small shops, exchanging nine for ten cigarettes, packing them in small bags or exchanging them loosely. However, less than a day after the exchange, they are inspected by Shanghai inspectors, who determine that they are counterfeit, and are detained and sent to the police for punishment. There have been several such cases every day. In order to protect against being deceived and punished, the office yesterday issued another notice to its members, stating: "We have learned that there are many brands of cigarettes sold by our colleagues. Recently, some unscrupulous elements have been falsely claiming to be company runners, coming to sell counterfeit 'Little Fairy' cigarettes and other brands. Although this office has issued three notices, some people have not paid attention and have been deceived and punished. Therefore, we are issuing an urgent notice. If there are cigarettes being sold door-to-door, we hope that shopkeepers will pay attention to avoid being deceived and fined. If anyone continues to sell the aforementioned counterfeit cigarettes in front of you, please pay attention and hand them over to the police. Otherwise, once caught, they will be subject to a large fine. Do not neglect and harm yourself. This is a crucial notice."

Alber Road: A Blood Case Occurred Last Night. A Chinese Employee of the Meifeng Store Was Shot and Killed by a Foreigner. 137

The Meifeng Tobacco and Alcohol Store and JOS'E Bar are both located at the intersection of Ya'erpei Road and Central Sports Field. A man named Li Mingshu, in his teens, worked as a waiter in JOS'E Bar. Yesterday around 8 PM, Li was sent by the store owner to buy something at Meifeng. He happened to meet Wu Xiaosizi, an employee of Meifeng, and since they were very familiar, they chatted casually. They teased each other in their words, but unexpectedly, Wu Xiaosizi became angry and slapped Li on the cheek. Li, being young, felt wronged and returned to the store with tears in his eyes, complaining to the store owner. It happened to be seen by a foreigner in the bar, who was already drunk. He stood up and forced Li Mingshu to go to Meifeng to negotiate. Unexpectedly, as soon as the foreigner entered Meifeng, he slapped Wu Xiaosizi on the cheek. Wu Xiaosizi tried to resist, but the foreigner immediately pulled out a self-defense pistol from his side and fired at Wu. Wu Xiaosizi saw this and quickly turned to avoid it, but it was too late. The bullet entered through his back and exited through his chest, and he immediately fell to the ground in the store. The police post was nearby, and hearing the gunshot, they rushed into the store to inquire. Seeing the situation, they immediately telegraphed the police station and notified the fire brigade to send Wu Xiaosizi to the hospital for treatment. However, the injury was fatal, and he soon died. The body was sent to the coroner's office for an autopsy. The foreigner who caused the accident and Li Mingshu were both taken into custody by the police.

The Shenhu Class Yuanfeng Steamer: Robbed Near Luxu. Passengers and Account Room Lost More Than a Thousand Dollars. The Company Has Asked the Association to Submit a Request to the Authorities for Strict Apprehension. 140

The Yuantong Shipping Bureau at 494 Beisuzhou Road has seven ships: Yuanxiang, Yuanji, Yuanyuan, Yuanfa, Yuantong, Yuanfeng, and Yuanchang, all of the Shenhu class. The Yuanfeng steamer left Shanghai for Huzhou at 11:30 AM on the 30th of last month. At 10:30 PM that night, when passing through Liujiagang, near Luxu, it was suddenly attacked by a large gang of bandits who fired guns and robbed the ship. The captain, forced by force, had no choice but to stop sailing. All thirty-odd passengers were not spared, and the silver dollars and clothes they carried were robbed, worth about seven or eight hundred dollars. The account room lost 500 paper dollars. The entire robbery lasted for about an hour, and then the bandits left with their loot. Once the bandits left, the captain continued sailing as usual. After arriving in Huzhou, he immediately telegraphed the report of the robbery. After the Pingwang Public Security Bureau received the alarm, it immediately dispatched water police to rush to the scene, but the bandits had already carried their loot far away. The Yuanfeng steamer returned to Shanghai yesterday morning, and the captain reported to the company in writing. The company immediately reported to the Inland Steamer Industry Association, telegraphing the competent authorities for strict apprehension. However, the Yuanfeng steamer still sailed from Shanghai to Huzhou as usual yesterday afternoon. (Note: This matter was already seen in yesterday's local news column, but the details were not clear, so it is recorded again.)

Zhejiang Local Bank Inspection Report 150

The 72nd inspection report of the Zhejiang Local Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: Members of this committee, along with the entrusted accountant, inspected the issuance reserve fund of the Zhejiang Local Bank in accordance with the rules of this committee. The 72nd inspection was held at the bank on September 30th, 24th year of the Republic of China. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 3,475,880 yuan and 5 jiao, including 2,984,845 yuan and 7 jiao in silver dollar coupons and 491,034 yuan and 8 jiao in fractional currency coupons. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve is 3,475,880 yuan and 5 jiao, including 2,524,720 yuan and 5 jiao in cash reserve of silver dollars and 951,160 yuan in secured reserve converted into silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Zhejiang Local Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, the issuance of exchange coupons shall have 60% as cash reserve and 40% as secured reserve. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve is above 70% and the secured reserve is below 30%, which is in compliance with the established regulations. This report is hereby submitted. September 30th, 24th year of the Republic of China. Representatives: Zhou Xiangxian of Zhejiang Provincial Government, Shi Xirong of Zhejiang Provincial Federation of Commerce, Xu Xinggong of Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce, Jin Guanxian and Chuan Ruihe of Hangzhou Banking Association, Jin Liansheng and Hu Gengyang of Hangzhou Money Dealers Association, Zhang Facheng and Wu Qiao, representatives of the board of directors of Zhejiang Local Bank, Accountant Han Zude.

Another Volume of Rare Literary Books Published: Striking the Table in Amazement 151

The Shanghai Magazine Company publishes the first edition of "Striking the Table in Amazement," the fourth part of the Rare Literary Books of China series. It consists of 36 volumes, written by Ling Mengchu of the Ming Dynasty. The "Three Words and Two Beats" is a comprehensive collection of Ming Dynasty novels, which was very popular at the time. After entering the Qing Dynasty, it was banned and lost circulation for a long time. Later generations only knew of the "Stories Old and New," which was selected and compiled, and no longer knew of the "Three Words and Two Beats." It can be said that they have forgotten their origins. The series aims to restore the old appearance at the cost of huge sums of money, collecting rare and good editions from various sources, carefully punctuating and proofreading them, and publishing them continuously. The complete book contains 400,000 words, divided into two thick volumes, and comes with a book cover for easy storage. It was published today. The retail price for the entire set is only 7 jiao. A special edition printed on thick pound Huangdaolin paper costs 1 yuan. Mail orders are postage-free. The series will continue to accept reservations for one month starting from the 1st of this month. The complete set includes 50 books, divided into 70 thick volumes. The popular edition costs 17 yuan, and the special edition costs 24 yuan. For out-of-town orders, add 1 yuan and 5 jiao for postage. On average, each book costs only a little over 3 jiao, which can be said to be extremely cheap. The reservation period ends at the end of this month. It is also heard that the books to be published this month include "Striking the Table in Amazement" (one volume), "Miscellaneous Notes from Xiqing" (one volume), "The Plum in the Golden Vase" (four volumes), and "Newly Transcribed Letters from Laigutang" (one volume), a total of four types. The second volume of "Liuting Poetry Talk," which was left over from last month, will also be released on the 19th, for a total of nine thick volumes, which is much busier than last month.

Ya Pu Er Factory Compiles and Prints Common Knowledge of Light Bulbs 154

Due to the slow typesetting of the printing house, it was only published today. The content is rich and the printing is exquisite. All sectors are welcome to request a copy free of charge. However, a letter with the seal of an organization or business firm is required in order to receive it.

Crime Statistics for Last Week in This City 155

The Municipal Public Security Bureau announced that a total of 286 criminal cases occurred within the city limits in the past week. A total of 508 male and female criminals were investigated and arrested, which are listed as follows: Robbery and aggravated robbery cases: 21 cases, 19 criminals; Theft cases: 71 cases, 103 criminals; Forgery cases: 46 cases, 89 criminals; Abduction cases: 33 cases, 58 criminals; Red pill and morphine cases: 12 cases, 32 criminals; Gambling cases: 5 cases, 23 criminals; Fraud cases: 20 cases, 29 criminals; Communist Party cases: 3 cases, 6 people; Homicide cases: 6 cases, 7 people; Fire cases: 8 cases, 10 people; Counterfeit money cases: 6 cases, 8 people; Violation of police regulations cases: 50 cases, 79 people; Other criminal cases: 13 cases, 45 people. Total: 286 cases, 508 people. All of the above-mentioned criminals were investigated and concluded by the Third Section. Except for minor cases, which were dealt with in accordance with the Regulations on Penalties for Violations of Police Regulations, or sentenced to release, and drug offenders who were ordered to sign a guarantee and obtain a license, totaling 74 people, the remaining criminals were sent to the local court or other competent authorities for trial. The number of criminal cases investigated and arrested this week increased by 4 cases compared to last week, and the number of criminals arrested increased by 36 people.

The Yangtze River Basin and the East China Sea: cloudy, gradually clearing, cooler, with morning fog and unstable northwest to northeast winds of varying degrees. Its center was located within approximately 60 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM. The wind strength is unknown. Another hurricane north of Guam is apparently moving northwest. Special Report: The Progress of the First Shanghai Literacy School (2) 158

A list of the number of classes and schools with students enrolled at the beginning of the first literacy school term

2. Inspection Situation: The inspection of the municipal literacy schools in this city is divided into three categories: 1. Inspection by the municipal government; 2. Inspection by the Municipal Literacy Education Committee; 3. Inspection by the offices of each district. The inspection by the municipal government is carried out by the staff of the municipal government. One inspection director is appointed for each literacy education district or several literacy education districts, for a total of 11 directors. In addition, more than 40 inspectors are appointed to be responsible for inspecting the literacy schools throughout the city. Each inspection director inspects for two weeks per term, and each inspector inspects for two to four weeks per term. All inspection situations are written into inspection reports and submitted to the mayor, who then forwards them to the Literacy Education Committee, which in turn informs the offices of each district and forwards them to each literacy school to improve operations. If there are too many student absences or poor order, the municipal government will also order the Public Security Bureau or its branches to correct or assist in correcting the situation. The inspection by the Municipal Literacy Education Committee is carried out by the executive officers of the committee. A total of inspections are carried out throughout the term. One is at the beginning of the term to inspect the opening situation of each school. One is in the middle of the term to inspect the attendance of students, check the number of students attending each school, and provide guidance on the school's general situation, facilities, teaching methods, moral education achievements, student situation reports, etc. The inspection by the offices of each district is carried out by the members of the academic affairs committees of each district. Except for the Zhonghua Confucian Temple and Pusong districts, which refer to and separately formulate forms, most adopt the Municipal Literacy Education Committee's inspection report form and inspect once to three times per month, and submit it to the Literacy Education Committee for verification at the end of the term. After the above three types of inspections, the final results are collected by the Municipal Literacy Education Committee for overall review and verification in order to unify authority. It is believed that the language, attitude, and teaching methods of the teachers are greatly related to the increase or decrease of students, but the literacy schools use the original schools or public places as school sites, and their facilities and environment are often inadequate, which affects the teaching performance. As for student absences, investigating and preparing reports and police summons are time-consuming and costly, which is also a major factor affecting teaching efficiency. (To be continued)

Sports News

Under Hu Wenhu's Leadership, Malaysian Chinese Athletes Returned to the Homeland Yesterday, the 150 Athletes are Formidable, Group Representatives Welcomed Them, An Unprecedented Grand Occasion, A Grand Tea Party Scheduled for Tomorrow in Shanghai 159

The delegation of Malaysian Chinese athletes and tourists, numbering 150, led by General Leader Hu Wenhu, arrived in Shanghai on the Italian ship "Conte Verde". They arrived at the China Merchants Bureau's North Wharf at 5:17 PM yesterday. Representatives from 97 groups, including the Municipal Education Bureau, Social Bureau, and Chamber of Commerce, as well as faculty and students from various schools and people from all walks of life, totaling about 14,000 people, went to welcome them. The atmosphere was warm and the scene was unprecedented. Details are recorded as follows:

A Glimpse Upon Arrival

At 5:17 PM, amidst the music of the Public Security Bureau's military band and the cheers of the welcoming crowd, the Italian ship docked at the pier. Representatives from the Education Bureau, Social Bureau, Aviation Association, and others, including Pan Gongzhan (representing Jiang Jianbai), Li Dachao, Xu Shiying, Hu Zongfan, Zhang Bingjun, and Yuan Zengyu representing the All-China Games reception group, as well as newspaper reporters Ma Chonggan, Zhuang Shunyuan, Xia Kaiming, and school principals Lu Lihua, Chen Mengxuan, Li Zhaohuan, and others, boarded the ship one after another, shaking hands with Hu Wenhu and others to express their welcome and deliver welcoming speeches. Ms. Xu Xu of the Chen Bao newspaper, as well as female students from Liangjiang and Guangdong, also presented flower baskets to express their enthusiasm. After the flower presentation, Hu Wenhu and the athletes disembarked together for a photo session, then boarded special buses led by the municipal government's large automobile to the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School for rest.

The Athletes' Appearance

The male Malaysian Chinese athletes participating in the All-China Games all wore gray flannel trousers, blue flannel tops, and grayish-white pith helmets. The female athletes wore gray wool qipaos with blue flannel, turn-down collar short shirts. General Leader Hu Wenhu and the male and female staff wore the same attire as the athletes, neat and beautiful, and their strong physique and lively spirit were particularly full of boundless vitality, inspiring people.

Presenting Flowers and Expressing Greetings

Representatives from various physical education groups in the city, including Li Dachao, presented flowers on the ship and delivered a welcoming speech on behalf of 97 groups, saying: "The Sixth National Games are held in Shanghai. More than 160 overseas Chinese athletes from Malaya, led by General Leader Mr. Hu Wenhu, Deputy Leaders Mr. Lin Jindian, and Mr. Wang Jingcheng, have arrived in Shanghai today, pioneering overseas Chinese compatriots participating in the motherland's grand gathering. This is truly a great undertaking. Mr. Hu, Lin and Wang are not only leaders of the overseas Chinese, but also care about the motherland and are particularly enthusiastic about social welfare and charitable causes, which have long been admired by the people of the country. This time, they have led young overseas Chinese from afar to return to the motherland to visit the country in addition to participating in the All-China Games, so that they can have a deep impression of the motherland's political construction, etc. Its significance is profound. Our association and other 97 groups jointly welcome you and present these humble words on the occasion of the arrival of the leaders and athletes in Shanghai to express our admiration. We hope you will remember this." Initiated by Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, China Aviation Association, Municipal Sports Association, Shen Bao Newspaper, Xinwen Bao Newspaper, Chen Bao Newspaper, Shi Bao Newspaper, Shanghai News Agency, Zao Bao Newspaper, Tianjin Dagong Bao Newspaper, Min Bao Newspaper, Shidai Ribao Newspaper, Shanghai Branch of the China Cultural Construction Association, Shanghai Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces, Shanghai YMCA, Chinese Vocational Education Society, Dongya Physical Education College, Liangjiang Normal School of Physical Education, China Basketball Students Association, Shanghai Art College, Shanghai Branch of Tiger Balm Yong An Tang, Shanghai Education Association, Diligent Physical Education Monthly Magazine, Guangdong Shanghai Association, China University, Jiaotong University, Guanghua University, and other 97 groups.

Hu Wenhu Speaks

Mr. Hu Wenhu expressed his views on participating in the All-China Games on the ship, saying: "This time, I, Wenhu, led the Malayan Chinese team back to the country to participate in the Sixth National Games, with nearly 150 male and female athletes and staff. It is the largest organization of overseas Chinese returning to the country for sightseeing in history. Although its surface purpose is the same as that of the provinces and cities participating, its significance seems to be slightly different. Now, I will briefly describe one or two of my humble opinions, and I hope that the people of the country will appreciate them. The physique of our people is weak, and we have been ridiculed as the 'sick men of East Asia.' I believe that if we want to revitalize the spirit of our nation, we should first strengthen the physique of our people. It is impossible to succeed without actively promoting sports. The holding of the All-China Games allows the athletes of the whole country to gather in one place, learn from each other, and promote sports. Its function is the greatest. Malayan Chinese sports are still in their infancy, so I, Wenhu, advocate that the number of selected participants should be large and that all sections should be equal, so that the athletes and staff who return to the country will not only improve their sports skills, but also use their gained experience in the future to develop the cause of sports. Their gains will be far from small. This is the first significance of the Malayan team returning to the country to participate in the All-China Games. Overseas Chinese have left the country for thousands of miles, and there is a great deal of separation from the situation in the motherland. Even among the athletes who have returned to the country this time, most of them are overseas Chinese students who have never set foot in the motherland. Now, taking advantage of the opportunity to participate in the All-China Games, they return to the country for sightseeing, so that they can have a deeper understanding of the motherland, which can communicate the voices of China and Southeast Asia and harmonize the feelings of inside and outside. This is the second significance of the Malayan team participating in the All-China Games. This All-China Games is held in Shanghai, which is the most cultural and historical area in our country. Culture, education, and other industrial and commercial industries are all the best in the country. In addition to the competition, the Malayan Chinese team will conduct various inspections. Their feelings and impressions will be good, and their gains will be considerable. This is another significance of the Malayan Chinese team participating in the All-China Games. As for the establishment of championships in the Games, it is a method to promote technology. Malayan Chinese sports have not been promoted for a long time, and their achievements are still immature. Victory is not something we dare to expect, and the championship is not the purpose of this trip. We only hope that the domestic talents will come forward to teach us, then it will be fortunate."

Ordinary Performance; Shanghai Wins Against British Inness; the 4-2 Situation Was Very Tense; More Effort Is Needed for the Football Championship 167

The Shanghai football team played its final practice match against the British Army Inness at Shen Garden yesterday afternoon, with the Shanghai players winning 4-2. In the first half, the Shanghai players took a 2-1 lead. Approximately 2,000 to 3,000 people watched.

MacFarlane Scores First

Shanghai kicked off first. For the first five minutes, the teams remained deadlocked, carefully watching each other, making it difficult to score. The British army suddenly launched an attack, and MacFarlane bravely took the lead, launching a solo attack on the Shanghai team's goal. It was too late to save, and the ball went into the net, leaving Zhang Rongcai helpless.

Jinshun Is Still Charming

Both sides fought fiercely. Cao Qiuting repeatedly dribbled deep, but the British defensive line was too strong and difficult to break through, and he was often intercepted. Sun Jinshun raised his arm and caught a pass from Li Yichen, kicking it forcefully. It was too late to save, and the ball went into the net. Sun's iron leg was indeed extraordinary.

Linjing Scores Lightly

British center MacFarlane repeatedly displayed his courage, launching solo attacks deep into the Shanghai defense. Fortunately, Feng Yunyou was stationed in the rear, handling the situation with ease and making it difficult for MacFarlane to achieve his goal. He was repeatedly intercepted. The British army, focusing solely on offense, neglected their defense, allowing Liang Shutang to attack on the left wing and pass the ball to Jia Youliang. Jia dribbled forward and crossed from the baseline, and Dai Linjing caught up and lightly tapped the ball into the net. The first half ended with Shanghai leading 2-1.

Jinshun Accomplishes Twice

Changing sides, the British Army bravely took the lead, launching a full-scale attack on the Shanghai line. Feng and Jiang tried their best to cope, but the center line was slightly weak, allowing the British army to frequently penetrate the inner defense line. Fortunately, Zhang Rongcai was willing to sacrifice himself, repeatedly saving dangerous balls. His selfless struggle was praised by the audience. However, this left the British Inness defense empty, and Dai Linjing dribbled through the British center line and entered the back defense line. It was Jinshun who made a strong shot, sending the ball into the net.

Kallen Returns a Goal

Less than ten minutes into the second half, it began to rain. The two sides continued to compete in the rain, without giving an inch. With Hall's help, Kallen returned a goal in the heavy rain, scoring successfully. Shanghai still led by two goals.

Iron Leg Scores Three Goals

For twenty minutes, the two sides engaged in a close battle, without any gains or losses. The audience cheered frequently, and the atmosphere was extremely tense. Amid the cheers, Jia dribbled forward, passing it directly to Sun Jinshun. Living up to the audience's expectations, he shot the ball into the goal, but it hit the crossbar and bounced back in. The whistle blew, and the fierce battle came to an end, with a final score of 4-1.

Shanghai's Performance Is Ordinary

In yesterday's match, British Inness showed much more improvement than in the past, frequently approaching the Shanghai goal. However, their center line was too weak and lacked stability. If the British Inness shots had been more accurate, there would have been a new situation. Furthermore, the Shanghai team's forwards lacked activity on the left and right wings, and the ball was mostly advanced through the center, which was not a perfect tactic and should be paid attention to. Based on yesterday's performance, the Shanghai team's prospects for winning the football championship at the National Games are not optimistic.

Little Boy (6)(7) 169

— Original by Mrs. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Ned heard and shouted, "Oh! Sir, where is he going?"

"To a pleasant place in the countryside. When children can't learn well here, I send them there. Mr. Bei is a kind-hearted man. If Tang En is willing to work hard and do well, he will encounter a happy life there."

"Can he come back again?" Little Bridge asked.

"That all depends on himself; I hope he can."

After Mr. Pei said this, he went to another room to write a letter to Mr. Bei, while the children all surrounded Tang En, as if he were about to embark on a dangerous journey to a remote and desolate area.

"I don't know if you will like that," Jie Ke began to say.

"Even if I don't like it, I won't stay anymore," Dian En said coldly, as if nothing could move his heart.

"Then where will you go?" Ned asked.

"I might go overseas or go to the Northwest to reclaim wasteland and see what the situation is like there," Tang En replied, speaking with a sense of indifference that made the little boys breathless.

"Oh, don't! Live with Mr. Bei for a while and then come back here; Tang En, be sure to come back," Ned pleaded, feeling deeply moved by the whole thing.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Leader 170

— Sen

A brand new, clean piece of clothing is put on, and after not many days, when you take it off and look closely, the other parts are still fine, but only the "collar" and "cuffs" are the dirtiest. When Mom washes them, she uses extra effort, so they are most easily damaged. This is of course also expected.

Originally, the "collar" holds the central position of the whole garment, with the sole responsibility of maintaining its main body. The "cuffs" move with the all-powerful hands, working the most, so it's no wonder they are the most easily soiled. However, because they are the most easily soiled, their duties are naturally the most important!

A piece of clothing cannot do without the "collar" and "cuffs." Even an organization, a group, cannot do without "leaders." Furthermore, a modern nation cannot do without excellent and outstanding "leaders" to lead the people and maintain its sole body - the nation - like a piece of clothing, even if they are soiled or damaged to the point of destruction, they remain silent and without complaint!

The Battle of Abyssinia and Adowa 171

— Pei Yu

In recent months, no major event has surpassed the conflict between Italy and Abyssinia.

We are very familiar with the name of Italy because of Mussolini, the black-shirted prime minister, a globally renowned eccentric. The name of Abyssinia, however, is very unfamiliar. It is an ancient black nation located in eastern Africa, also known as Ethiopia. It is one of the three independent countries in Africa, with an area of ​​1.12 million square kilometers and a population of about 10 million. It has rich mineral resources and land suitable for cultivation and animal husbandry. The export volume of wax, ivory, and coffee is very large. The current king is Haile Selassie. Although Abyssinia is located near the Red Sea and the Indian Ocean, it is completely isolated from the ocean because it is surrounded by the territories of the United Kingdom, France, and Italy. From this, we can also imagine the complexity of its international relations.

Now, the disputes between Italy and Abyssinia not only cannot be resolved, but are becoming more profound, and the war has already broken out. The Italian army has 250,000 troops stationed in Eritrea, an Italian colony in northern Abyssinia, and in Italian Somaliland in eastern and southeastern Abyssinia. As for Abyssinia, it has expressed a very brave attitude towards Italy's aggression and oppression. The King of Abyssinia has repeatedly stated that Abyssinia must guarantee its own independence. He said, "We would rather die for freedom than live as slaves!" These are such brave words!

Abyssinia has hope. Although it has been placed on the chopping block to be slaughtered, it inflicted a huge blow on Italy 39 years ago (1896). As long as it can maintain its previous glory and make a final struggle, even if it perishes, it will be very glorious.

Thirty-nine years ago, the now prominent Mussolini was only twelve years old and was learning socialist theories from his blacksmith father. The Battle of Adowa began at this time. At that time, the Italian army had a total of 20,000 people, half of whom were local indigenous reinforcements. They advanced in three teams on the left, right, and center, and there was another team to provide support in the rear. Each team was commanded by a general. First, the Italian army occupied the two ridges facing Adowa. Later, the Abyssinian soldiers charged forward one after another, and the Italian army's cannons could not stop their advance. As a result, the entire Italian army was annihilated; two generals, 252 officers, and 4,500 soldiers were killed, 45 officers, and 1,500 soldiers were captured, and all the cannons were completely seized by the Abyssinian soldiers.

Children! What are your thoughts after hearing this story?
