Fried Mixed Vegetable 173

— Zhen

Fried mixed vegetable is a common dish that Min'er often eats for breakfast because he finds it crispy and fragrant.

But he likes to eat it very much, but doesn't know what it is made of? And how can it be crispy? Even if he looks through books, there is no record related to it.

"Dad, how is fried mixed vegetable made? Can you tell me?" He quickly ran to his dad to ask him.

"Is it fried mixed vegetable? Have you ever paid attention to when they make it in the shop on the street?"

"I haven't paid attention, I thought it was easy and not worth much."

"That's your mistake. I often say to you: "You must pay attention to everything, especially the smallest things." Since you don't know, I will tell you:

Fried mixed vegetable is made of wheat flour, but how does it become crispy? It is made by mixing alum and baking soda. Crispness is a chemical change, which is very mysterious, and you probably won't understand it.

Prepare a bowl of cold clean water, dissolve the alum in the clean water, and then dissolve the baking soda and salt in the water, stirring with a stick so that they are completely dissolved. At this time, there will be many bubbles in the bowl. Blow away the bubbles, and the clean water in the bowl will turn milky white. This milky white water is called fermented water. Then, put the very fine wheat flour in a shallow basin, pour the fermented water in, and continuously knead and mix it by hand. At this time, the wheat flour has become a paste. Then, put it on a board, make it into strips, and then cut it into small strips with a knife. Stack the two small strips together, gently press them with a wooden stick, pinch the ends with your fingers and stretch them out, and then twist them into spiral strips. Fry them in a vegetable oil pot, and after a while, they will expand and become golden brown fried mixed vegetable."

"Dad, what are alum and baking soda?"

"Alum is very similar to rock candy, and it can make dirty water clean. Baking soda helps digestion."

The Little Teachers of the Newspaper-Selling Children's Work-Study Group 174

— Ouyang Gu

Newspaper-selling children are our most pitiful little friends! They lost their education at a young age and sell newspapers to others to read, but they can't understand the newspapers they sell. Of course, they are also willing to study, but it is a pity that there is no one to teach them. Going to noble schools is simply out of the question. Now, there is a very good news. I think the little friends are very willing to hear and support it! That is, on Weisai Road in this city, east of the little vegetable market, a "Newspaper-Selling Children's Work-Study Group" school has been established. The slogan written on the white oil green background sign at the school gate: If you study, you will be able to read the newspaper, come if you want to study! And can you read the newspaper yourself after selling it to others? These are very eye-catching slogans.

Speaking of the establishment of this small cultural cell, it was originally due to the collective efforts of the newspaper-selling children in that area. At first, they had classes in the open air in an alley, with four literate newspaper-selling children as little teachers. In less than two weeks, they had finished reading four volumes of Old and Young Tong. Later, the newspaper-selling children conflicted with each other due to work hours and the climate. They had to wait until after ten o'clock in the morning before they could finish selling newspapers, and they had to sell newspapers before five o'clock in the evening. All the spare time was during the time when the sun was hanging high, so they asked the neighboring literate schools in the area for assistance and rented that school house for six yuan a month. Inside, there are three Eight Immortals tables, covered with long boards. The stools are rented temporarily. Maps; blackboards and lead powder are all donated, and the books are distributed by literate schools. The four little teachers take turns volunteering to teach. They rely on selling newspapers for food, and isn't it a full study in both work and learning to seek some new wisdom every day? Moreover, in this small Work-Study Group school, they can take the spare time to study with peace of mind. Now their scope is expanding and expanding, and the number of members has increased to more than 70. There are seven little teachers in charge of the Children's Work-Study Group, and the Advanced Citizen Textbook will also be finished reading. Many of the members have already learned to read the newspapers they sell!

Orangutan Sitting in a Sedan 175

— Schoolteacher

Orangutans are a type of monkey. Among animals, they are considered the smartest. Although their intelligence and ingenuity are not as good as humans, their claws and teeth are more powerful than those of humans. If people want to catch live orangutans, they cannot hope to catch them empty-handed. Therefore, they use the orangutan's nature of loving imitation to trick them into catching them.

Once, a traveler traveled in the mountains by sedan. Halfway there, the traveler got out of the sedan and walked, looking at the scenery. The sedan bearers were tired and rested, sitting on the mountain rocks dozing off. Unexpectedly, a few orangutans, taking advantage of the people's unpreparedness, jumped down from the trees. Some squeezed into the sedan and sat, pretending to be guests, while others learned from the sedan bearers, carrying the sedan, running and jumping crookedly. By the time the people woke up, they had already thrown the sedan far away.

One of the sedan bearers had an idea. The next day, he invited a few hunters, brought wine and food, and carried a few sedans. They put working locks on the sedan doors and passed by the same place. They deliberately stopped the sedans, drank wine, and dispelled boredom. After a while, they deliberately left the wine and food there and wandered around.

When those orangutans saw that the people were gone and the sedans were empty, and the smell of wine was fragrant, they rushed forward and ate the remaining wine and food until they were drunk. Some walked into the sedan doors, either sitting or squatting. Some then came to close the sedan doors and carried the sedan to walk.

The waiting hunters suddenly shouted, and the orangutans were frightened and at a loss. Some fell down, and some ran away. Only the orangutans sitting in the sedans, unable to open the doors or jump out, had no choice but to be caught by the hunters.

This is also called "It's easy to get on stage, but it's hard to get off"!

Children's Education Comics

— Edited by Lotte Zhaifu, Illustrated by Zhang Youjian

(A) One of Health Education...Physical Examination 176

Explanation

(1) Mei Sheng is the older brother, very obese. His younger brother, Lan Sheng, is relatively thin. The two brothers are very close.

(2) One day, their mother said: I'm worried that your bodies are so different, one fat and one thin. It's best to have a doctor examine you.

(3) They walked hand in hand. Mei Sheng walked very fast, but Lan Sheng felt very tired and out of breath.

(4) When they arrived at the clinic, they took off their clothes. Feng Sheng examined Mei Sheng's lungs. Lan Sheng stared blankly. He didn't know what this was for.

(5) The doctor weighed them. The older brother weighed seventy-five pounds, and the younger brother only weighed thirty-two pounds.

(6) The doctor said: You are twelve years old and weigh seventy-five pounds, and he is nine years old and weighs only thirty-two pounds. One fat and one thin, neither meets the standards. You must pay attention to nutrition and exercise. Otherwise, it will be difficult to develop. These words made the two brothers anxious!

A Good Time for Reading in Autumn 177

— Ziming

A gust of cool wind suddenly flies in, announcing to us that "Autumn" has arrived in the world. What joyful news this is! The azure sky, set off by clouds like fish scales, reveals its serene grandeur even more, and our hearts become open and broad.

The autumn insects chirp and hum, as if they are reading diligently; children, with such good weather, shouldn't you be studying hard? Don't miss the opportunity; a little delay, and the bone-chilling winter will be here, followed by the sultry summer, and then the wearisome spring will follow closely behind. Quickly seize this lovely autumn and study hard.

How can we read to achieve the best results? When we read a piece of writing, we must at least connect it with speaking, composition, and writing; in this way, we can read the book, be able to speak about it, write it down, and even create something new. If we only get to the point of humming and chanting, then reading is just a pastime!

The greatest purpose of reading is to 'seek the truth'. When we read, we must find the candies in the book; these candies, when we eat them, are beneficial in every way and without a single drawback. The more we eat, the better the taste; the better the taste, the more we want to eat. The more we eat, the more we benefit, and we will become useful members of society.

Normally, we should read quietly, not aloud; in terms of practicality and efficiency, silent reading is more valuable than reading aloud, and this is something to pay attention to. Children, the great autumn has arrived, quickly study hard!

A Sleeping Beauty in Chicago 178

— Te

There is a young girl in Chicago, USA, named Man Jujian, who has been in a dream world for three and a half years, hence the title "Sleeping Beauty." She has been sleeping in a daze for years, and it is still a scientific mystery. She is under the special care of her loving mother. She contracted sleeping sickness in 1932 and struggled hard, and has only recently regained some awareness, but her mental activity is still minimal. According to her mother, her daughter's eyes can now be open for most of the day, and she can extend her fingers to answer questions about numbers, but there is no cure for this disease, so there is no certainty as to when she will fully recover. However, this loving mother does not give up hope. She told a news reporter: "My daughter's condition has improved a lot. She is making slow progress now. Her body is not as heavy as it used to be. She seems to be able to hear sounds, taste flavors, and feel pain." It is reported that the lady was twenty-six years old when she fell ill, and she is now twenty-nine years old. She began to catch a cold while lying on a train on January 19, 1932, but did not fall into a completely comatose state until mid-February. According to biologists, her nervous system has not been greatly damaged because her heart is still able to control her. This mother waits patiently, hoping day after day, recording the changes in the dream world in a small notebook every day, so that she can review it with her beautiful daughter in the future. She hopes and believes that one day she can hand this little notebook to her beloved daughter, who will be free from the shackles of the sleeping demon and as quick-witted as ever.

Good Girl 179

— Ning Ziqiang

There was a girl from a foreign country who happened to live next to the railway tracks. Not far from her residence was an iron bridge, a necessary passage for trains.

One day, a storm struck and the bridge was damaged. She thought that when the train arrived, it would be in an unknown and dangerous situation. Her small heart felt extremely uneasy.

She decided to light a torch and shout and wave on this side of the bridge. When the train arrived, they heard the commotion and knew that something had happened, so they stopped the train. After investigation, they found out that the bridge was broken. This good girl saved the lives of the passengers on the train.

The "New Yin" Ship Sank 180

— He Gongchao

A group of merchants took many goods and boarded a sea ship to do business overseas. At first, they were very harmonious, but later, some people advocated going to the northern seas, saying that the business there was very good and they could definitely make a lot of money; others advocated going to the southern seas, saying that the natives there needed their goods very much, and that the prices were high and the goods were easy to sell, so they could definitely make a lot of money. The two sides started with verbal disputes, and then turned to physical fights; the wind and waves grew bigger and bigger, and as a result, the helmsman dropped the rudder, the oarsmen threw down the oars, and everyone ran in a swarm to the deck, joining the battle and fighting together. They also ran to the cargo hold to increase their fighting strength, opened the wine that was going to be sold, and gulped it down. After drinking, they ran back to the deck to brawl. They fought desperately, each trying to kill the other, and no one was willing to give up. However, they left the ship, which everyone entrusted their lives to, to drift with the wind and run into hidden reefs.

While they were fighting, the weather suddenly changed. The sky was as dark as ink, lightning flashed like threads, and a violent wind roared and heavy rain poured down. The drifting ship was thrown into the air by the raging waves for a moment, and then pressed to the bottom of the waves for another. But these drunkards were still fighting! Suddenly, it seemed as if the sky and the earth had collapsed, and there was a loud noise. The ship hit a reef! The bow of the ship was broken by the reef, and water rushed in headlong...

At this time, a young man who had not drunk saw this scene and hurriedly ran to cover the hole with his hands; but with the water pouring in like this, how could one person's strength be enough to cover it? So he shouted loudly: "The ship is sinking! Everyone stop fighting!... Come... Come and save us..." But these drunkards were fighting vigorously on the deck, who would pay attention to him!

Soon, more and more water flooded the young man's thighs, and he became more and more anxious, shouting: "If you don't come to save us, the ship will sink immediately!..." But these drunkards were fighting vigorously on the deck, who would pay attention to him!

The young man had just shouted the last two words "sink" when the water had already flooded his chest. He shouted miserably: "You... You... If you don't... the ship... immediately..." He shouted to this point, the water poured into his throat, and at the same time the ship sank into the water, sank down..., and the people on the deck also sank down, sank down; but other than those who had already been beaten to death, the living people were still twisted together, fighting desperately...

The Story of the White Mountain Crow (4) 181

— Xi

After listening, he began to speak, saying: "If you were like me, a carrier pigeon, then you wouldn't have all these troubles. We only know how to travel, that is our life. We also have our love, but I don't know who my father is. Day after day, we break through the air and pass through space, watching the high mountains and plains all arranged under our feet. What we breathe is the pure air of the sky, not the turbid air of the ground. When we fly, we are like an arrow, straight to our destination, without making mistakes. This is our entertainment and also our life. The distance I travel in one day, humans can't catch up with me in ten days."

After listening to his words, I immediately became brave and said to him: "Sir, in that case, you are a wandering bird!"

The carrier pigeon replied: "This is not something I need to worry about. I have no homeland; I only know three things: my journey, my wife, and my children. Where my wife is, that is where my homeland is."

"But what is that hanging around your neck? It looks like a tattered piece of wrinkled paper."

The carrier pigeon replied, exhaling: "This is a very important document. This time I am going to Bai Luosai to bring a letter to the famous banker Mr. X, causing the currency price to fall by seven jiao eight fen in francs."

I cheered: "Great! Your life is really great, and that Bai Luosai city, I think it must be a city worth seeing. Can you take me with you? I am not a mountain crow, so maybe I am a carrier pigeon."

The carrier pigeon said: "If you were a carrier pigeon, then I just pecked you, and you have to peck me back."

"Sir, I can give it back to you; let's not argue over these small things. Look, the dawn is about to break. The storm has subsided. Please let me follow you! I have failed. I have nothing in this world; if you refuse me, then I will have to drown in this lake."

The carrier pigeon quickly said: "Very good, move forward, quickly move forward, as long as you can keep up with me, then come with me."

I took one last look at the garden where my mother was sleeping. A teardrop rolled out of my eyes; and it was immediately carried away by the wind and rain. I spread my wings and set off immediately.

I said long ago that my wings were not very strong yet. The guiding carrier pigeon flew like splashing wind, and I followed beside him, constantly panting; I tried for a while, but soon I felt a violent dizziness, almost fainting. I let out a weak voice and asked, "Is it still a long way to go"?

He replied: "Not far, we are already in Bao Yede; now we just need to hurry another hundred and eighty miles."

Grain – No Intention to Ship Foodstuffs from This Port – Mistaken for a 100-Ton Transshipment of Raw Peanuts – Actual Shipment Only 400 Tons 189

Yesterday, various Chinese and Western newspapers in this port widely reported that 100 tons of foodstuffs would be loaded onto an Italian ship bound for Italy. Yesterday, this newspaper believed there might be some truth to the rumor and proceeded to investigate further. The so-called 100 tons of foodstuffs turned out to be a mistaken report about 100 tons of raw peanuts being shipped from Qingdao to Shanghai for transshipment to Italy. Furthermore, it was discovered that the Italian ship "Kang Tie Fan Tian" scheduled to depart for Italy on the 9th will only be carrying around 400 tons of cargo from Shanghai. Besides the 100 tons of raw peanuts, there are also 95 tons of almonds being transshipped from Tianjin, 20 tons of miscellaneous goods being transshipped from Hankou, and over 200 tons of cargo being transshipped from Japan. There are no foodstuffs being shipped out from this port. (Editor's Note: Raw peanuts fall under the category of miscellaneous grains, which may have caused the confusion.)

Women's Realm

Revelry and Bizarre Costumes 193

— Like Hong

Recent newspaper reports said, "This year's Double Tenth Festival, Guangdong has organized revelry." And "During the Double Tenth Festival, the ban on bizarre costumes will be lifted..." This seems quite novel this year.

However, I feel that this "novelty" is abnormal. In these times of national turmoil and escalating global crises, not only the poor Chinese people have no reason to rejoice, but even the so-called powerful capitalist countries and other small nations are suffering intensely.

The word "revelry" ("歡") has "madness" ("狂") above it. "Madness" is an adjective describing abnormality. Trying to "rejoice" without "joy" is like a dying person saying, "I want to live" at the moment of death. Therefore, it is not surprising that there is "revelry" just before the Second World War.

With revelry, the "ban on bizarre costumes" will naturally be lifted. Otherwise, if the young ladies wear plain clothes, unable to expose their jade arms or bare their breasts, the revelry will be less interesting!

However, only a few can participate in revelry and wear bizarre costumes. The vast majority of women, unable to attend to such things, not only do not revel, not only do not wear bizarre costumes, but barely have time to mend old clothes, even frowning.

So, let those who want to revel, revel. Let those who want to wear bizarre costumes, wear them. Anyway, these are just the last excitements.

Her Way Out 194

— Luo Qiong

This magazine's previous issue carried Mr. Tie Huai's article "Where is Her Way Out," which recounted the dispute involving Mr. Jia, a "journalist turned middle school teacher" in Hangzhou, who seduced three women, A, B, and C. Now, Ms. B has been abandoned, leading to "no way out." This phenomenon is increasingly common in today's society. It is no longer just "an abnormal phenomenon in an abnormal society" but has become a widespread and serious problem in today's society. Examples include the sensational "Teng Bian Love Killing Case" in Beiping not long ago and the scandalous affair involving a certain inspector of the Shandong Education Bureau. Although the circumstances may not be identical, the underlying causes are similar. Therefore, we need to analyze and criticize these facts in detail.

Undoubtedly, the protagonist who created this situation is Mr. Jia. He took advantage of his position as a middle school teacher, "and taught female students. He used this to get to know many young women whose affections were just beginning to blossom. Because he was good at chatting and joking during class, he gained the favor of several young ladies." He repeatedly seduced women. First, he placed a "flower-like beauty" Ms. Nei—an unofficial Mrs. Jia, in his home to serve as his reproductive machine. Later, he used sweet words to flatter Ms. B repeatedly. When Ms. B was heavily pregnant, she discovered Jia's relationship with Ms. D. This kind of man, using his superior social position, repeatedly tramples on the weak woman whose affections were just blossoming" under the mask of "love," is already shocking. What's more, Mr. Jia is a "middle school teacher." Instead of taking responsibility for guiding students, he used this opportunity to carry out his seduction. This not only destroys women, but also destroys female education, giving opponents of female education more excuses, which is what makes us gnash our teeth in hatred the most.

As for the three women, A, B, and C, who were trampled on, Mr. Tie Huai did not reveal the situation of the latter two in detail, so we can only focus on the facts of Ms. B. Ms. B is an orphan who lost her parents early and has no siblings. Her only uncle, due to disputes over inheritance, damaged family affection and lost her support. In this vast and bleak situation, Mr. Jia first helped her fight for the inheritance, then repeatedly provided assistance, accompanied her to the hospital when she was sick, and left her at home to recuperate after her illness, and introduced her to a job. In this way, a young girl who had not experienced much of the world and was "friendless" and "suffering from illness" was naturally easily deceived by Mr. Jia's cunning plot. So we say that Ms. B's seduction was indeed understandable.

However, when Ms. B was moved to tears and surrendered her body, she at least neglected the following two points: First, Ms. B already knew that Ms. C had been living with Mr. Jia for many years and already had children. At this time, she should have first investigated the relationship between Jia and C. If Jia and C still had love for each other until then, then Ms. B should definitely not sacrifice Ms. Nei for her own desires. If there was no longer any love between Jia and C, then they should cohabitate after Jia and C's relationship was settled. Second, since Ms. B discovered Jia and D's relationship when she was heavily pregnant, Mr. Jia's attitude was already clearly visible. At this time, Ms. B should no longer have waited and seen, but should have cleared up her relationship quickly. But Ms. B was still dreaming of "resolving the Ms. D incident so that the child in her womb would have a legitimate father." Therefore, Mr. Jia's departure seemed so unexpected. Due to these two points of improper handling, Ms. B cannot completely shirk responsibility for her current "no way out."

However, here we should recognize clearly that although the occurrence of the facts is due to the four of them, the reason why this fact is allowed to happen has to be traced back to its social origins. In this male-centered society, men occupy all the advantages, so Mr. Jia can repeatedly seduce women and still remain at large. On Ms. B's side, her being seduced is first and foremost because she cannot be economically independent, and society does not provide any protection, so she has to rely on marriage as a profession and the only way to guarantee her life. Also, after she was abandoned, instead of realistically seeking a way out in society, she just sighed, "Will anyone be willing to marry me?" This also shows her fundamental attitude of "love is life, love is everything."

Therefore, to fundamentally eliminate these multi-party love disputes and enable both men and women to develop on normal paths, only after the fundamental reform of this male-centered society and the complete elimination of the obstacles to women's liberation, circling around the individual alone cannot achieve a thorough solution. However, it must be said again that before the thorough reform of the social system is realized, we cannot ask Ms. B to wait day after day. We must find a more reasonable way out within the possible range. According to Ms. B's current situation, on the negative side, we should first try to settle her relationship with Mr. Jia. It is better to treat him as an enemy and thoroughly settle it, and do not harbor any illusions and follow the wrong path of the past. On the positive side, it is to strive for an independent position in society. First of all, we should seek considerable independence in economic terms. In today's society, finding a job in general is very difficult, but Ms. B must never be disheartened because she is a "junior high school graduate." In Chinese society, it is truly rare for a woman to receive junior high school education. Even if she "has no connections" and cannot find a suitable job, doing street vending or hard labor is better than living a parasitic life of prostitution. What Ms. B is particularly reluctant to give up is "remarrying." This way out is just repeating the mistakes of the past. If Ms. B continues to use marriage as a profession or make love the center of her life, then no one can guarantee that she will not be deceived again. Therefore, "love" turning into "marriage" should be taken as a side issue here, and she should put most of her energy into social undertakings, especially awakening other young women who are still dreaming, in order to reform this unreasonable social system for the sake of relieving the shackles of oneself and all oppressed compatriots. If Ms. B can resolutely move forward in this direction, then although she will have to go through many hardships, I dare to say that Ms. B's future is still bright. And one day, she will despise this shameful and false "gentle dream" and receive greater comfort among the vast sisterhood!

Going Home (Continued) 195

— Su Hong

(Eight)

The night's panic frightened Mrs. Zhonggui into illness. Although young master Zhonggui was not sick, his cheeks were noticeably thinner. Relatives from nearby villages and clansmen, including the village head, came to offer condolences and visit.

"Old lady, you must drink some honeysuckle soup. Here is a package of ginseng. Have the maid boil it for you. Otherwise, I think it's better to send them (ghosts) away." The female relative said in a low voice.

The male guests were all in the living room. The village head clasped his hands and said with a smile:

"Congratulations! Congratulations! Brother Zhonggui! At least nothing was moved. As for the old lady's fright, a doctor will be called to take a look and she will be fine soon."

"Thank you! Thank! You! It is good that everyone is here. I originally wanted to ask everyone to discuss it."

Young master Zhonggui wanted to discuss two things: One was that when the fire first started last night, a robber took advantage of the situation to escape down the mountain and was caught by the militia. He is now tied up under the camphor tree, and it is not known how to deal with him. The other was that the fire last night destroyed seven or eight houses, creating a crowd of refugees, and it is not known how to deal with them in the best way.

Regarding the matter of the robber, everyone said in unison that he must be tortured to avoid future troubles. As for the refugees, that was a bit difficult, and everyone pondered. After eating ten plates of "pot" pastries, and also drinking a lot of ham soup, they still couldn't find a good solution.

"This matter can be discussed slowly. It is not good to have many refugees in the village. In short, find a way to maintain order in the area and prevent any disasters." Everyone said goodbye and left.

The ice in the river had turned into chunks, and the ice floes were covered with burnt ashes. The bank was a burnt field. Although the fire had been extinguished, green smoke still permeated the sky. Blackened beams and pillars were lying horizontally or hanging down, and tiles and broken bricks decorated the ruins. Someone discovered that a person had been burned to death and dug out from the pile of tiles and bricks. There were no clothes or hair, just a pitch-black segment.

"Who is it?" Mother asked. "That must be Aunt Youfu, alas, burned to death like this." She clasped her hands and bowed to the charred body several times. Shedding tears, she said to Lifu's wife, "We've been good friends for so many years. I didn't think she would die like this... I knew something was wrong. There was a 'bang' sound. The bodhisattva foretold me. Look at this, how can we not worship the bodhisattva!"

"What bodhisattva, no bodhisattva. I won't. If he is spiritual, why didn't he protect us from being burned?"

"Mother! Don't say that. Now that we've gotten to this point, we're all relying on the bodhisattva to protect us. God, don't blame her for not understanding!" Just as the sister-in-law was about to retort, a person was seen hanging from the elm tree. The little nun came to report that they were going to beat the robber. She dragged Xiuzhen to see. The robber's two big toes were tied tightly with two hemp ropes. His feet were not touching the ground, and two stones were hung on them. His whole body was straight as a line, moving in the air. Young master Zhonggui's attendants, awakened by the liquor, bared their chests and beat him with a tree branch with all their might. After hitting a few times, they asked:

"Tell me, who is your leader?"

The robber did not say anything. After being tortured again, they asked:

"Tell me quickly, who is your leader?"

The robber still did not say anything. At first, he screamed and yelled, but later gradually turned into a "mhm mhm" humming.

Young master Zhonggui gave the order, saying that he had to be made to speak, and that they would not stop beating him if he did not speak. (To be continued)

Legal Advice 196

(Question) I am cohabitating with Mr. A, but we have not held a wedding ceremony. However, Mr. A is already married to Ms. B, and we obtained Ms. B's consent before moving in together. We lived harmoniously for half a month, but now Ms. B's family has suddenly become opposed to it and is inciting others to threaten me. I would be grateful if you could answer the following questions.

(1) Does Ms. B's family have the right to interfere with our cohabitation? Is our cohabitation legal?

(2) Can Mr. A be charged with bigamy or any other crime?

(3) If Ms. B does not file a lawsuit, can others file a lawsuit?

(4) If Mr. A abandons me, can I obtain reasonable living expenses? -Yi Ying

(Answer)

(1) No.

(2) Since no wedding ceremony was held, the crime of bigamy is not established. However, if the cohabitation continues after the implementation of the new criminal law on July 1st, Mr. A will be in violation of Article 239 regarding interference with marriage, and the woman is equally culpable.

(3) No. The crime under Article 239 requires prosecution upon complaint. Ms. B, having condoned it beforehand, cannot bring charges, but her consent must be reliably proven.

(4) If the woman's union with Mr. A is not merely an ambiguous cohabitation relationship but implies permanent cohabitation as a member of the family (i.e., obtaining the status of a concubine), then if Mr. A abandons the woman without cause, causing her to fall into financial hardship, she may request reasonable alimony.

(Question)

(1) If a husband and wife are estranged, and the husband has been away for several years and does not return, making the wife a de facto widow, can she file a lawsuit?

(2) If an aunt raises a niece from childhood until she is about to marry, but then sends her home and disregards her completely, as if severing the relationship, can the niece file a lawsuit to divide the adoptive mother's property? (If the adoptive mother does not acknowledge the adoptive daughter, what can be done?) Or are there other solutions?

(3) If an aunt raises a ten-year-old niece (who is fatherless) for one or two years, can she freely give her away? If a girl in her teens is adopted, can procedures be put in place to prevent her future abandonment? If she is taken in as an adopted daughter, but in the future, she is intended to be the son's wife, can this be implemented? How can it be prevented? -You Zhen

(Answer)

(1) She can request cohabitation.

(2) An adoptive relationship can be terminated by mutual consent at any time. If the adoptive mother has engaged in malicious abandonment as stipulated in Article 1081, Section 2 of the Civil Code, the adoptive daughter may sue for termination of the adoptive relationship, and if she is faultless and falls into financial hardship, she may request the payment of appropriate support. Whether she is actually an adoptive daughter must be proven by the plaintiff.

(3) The adoption of children should be done in writing, except in cases where the child has been raised as one's own from a young age. Furthermore, betrothal and marriage should be based on the free will of the man and woman involved; others should not force them. If a marriage contract is arranged by parents on behalf of their children when they are young, and the daughter does not wish to ratify it after she comes of age, she can sue for a declaration of invalidity. (Lawyer Pu Shunqing)

Women's Issues Forum

Section 4: Occupational Issues 197

The occupational issue for women is similar to the issues of political participation and education: it concerns women gaining equal rights with men in the workplace. The content of this issue includes demands for equal pay for equal work, protection of motherhood, the opening of all occupational sectors, and the abolition of all gender-based discrimination in employment. Many people in our country who care about women's issues have engaged in heated discussions on this topic. However, the general understanding of the essence of this issue is still insufficient. Especially after the recent outbreak of the global economic panic, this issue has not only failed to be further resolved but has instead given rise to various disputes. Therefore, I feel it is still necessary to raise this issue for discussion.

The occupational issue for women is also an inevitable product of the growth process of capitalist society. After capitalism broke down the feudal system, it reorganized all social matters according to its own needs, making them suitable for its development. A train speeding across the mountains and an airplane flying through the sky are certainly suitable for the growth of capitalism, and a politician tirelessly campaigning and a farmer toiling in the fields are also suitable for the development of capitalism. Similarly, a female office worker busy typing in an office or a female shop assistant busy serving customers in a department store is also suitable for the existence and development of capitalism. In other words, everything in capitalist society is very suitably arranged and organized to increase the profits of capitalists. The so-called female worker has also emerged to meet this need.

The so-called working woman, in a broad sense, refers to all women who sell their mental or physical labor in exchange for a livelihood, including female laborers. In a narrow sense, it refers to female employees or business owners with some administrative or technical abilities who have independent status. The term "working woman" usually refers to the latter, and therefore, this discussion will focus on the latter.

The specific reasons for the emergence of working women can be observed from two aspects. On the one hand, the capitalist mode of production requires not only large-scale economic production organizations but also huge consumption and distribution mechanisms. In order to increase their profits, the bourgeoisie wants to operate this huge social mechanism in the most agile and economical way. Therefore, female technicians who are agile, hard-working, and require very cheap labor conditions have become their target of need. On the other hand, the capitalist mode of production has gradually destroyed the old family economy and family system, while turning all members of society into two types of people: those who live off profits and those who live off wages. Most men who rely solely on wages are unable to support their wives or daughters, and their wives or daughters must also become wage earners who sell their physical or mental labor. Due to these two fundamental reasons, the number of working women has been increasing day by day, and the issue of working women has become a major social problem, even becoming a central issue in the women's liberation movement.

In Europe and the United States, this issue has been a matter of general concern since the early 19th century. During the rise of capitalism, although women had to seek employment in society, society also needed female workers. However, women faced many difficult struggles to enter the workplace. Male-dominated society was relatively lenient in opening up the lowest levels of physical labor to women, but it was unwilling to easily open up the higher levels of mental labor. That is to say, male-dominated society viewed it as normal for a woman to be a factory worker, as if women could only do that kind of low-level work. But if she wanted to be a female doctor or a female teacher, many arguments would be raised, saying that women having careers would be a factor in destroying families, a root cause of disrupting social order, and that women were inherently inferior and could not handle important social matters, and so on. Recently, there has been a similar phenomenon in our country, that is, in order to exclude working women, they are given the most demeaning name of "flower vases," especially in the Guangzhou male-female occupational dispute, where the male side raised the issue of social order to exclude women. Despite this, the historical mission of capitalism is bound to open up the future of women's careers. According to recent estimates, there are about 100 million working women in the world, and the United States alone already has 10 million, of which at least 10% are so-called working women in the narrow sense. According to the "Japan Labor Yearbook of Taisho 10," the total number of working women in Japan (there were 3.56 million female workers) was 865,078. Among them, 218,958 were engaged in the medical and pharmaceutical fields, education, and government offices, 605,793 were engaged in the commercial sector, 10,727 were engaged in the industrial sector, and 29,600 were engaged in other occupations. These are the figures from more than ten years ago, and the current number is certainly higher. Although there are no verifiable figures for working women in our country, it can be asserted that their numbers are increasing day by day.

In the midst of this increasing number of working women, capitalist society experienced internal flaws. Since 1929, an irreparable global economic panic broke out. In order to save themselves from the chaos of the panic, the bourgeoisies of various countries implemented fascist policies of domination, and these policies immediately affected the issue of women's employment. That is to say, in order to alleviate the panic of unemployment, countries were forcing women to return from the workplace to the home and replacing them with unemployed men, and thus working women suffered an unprecedented blow. Recently, some people in our country have also advocated that women's natural duty is to be wives and mothers and have rejected women's employment. This is also the same attempt by the general ruling class to oppress women in the total collapse of the entire capitalist economy! However, we must know that this is their last attempt, a temporary blow. History is bound to open up the future for working women and is bound to solve the issue of women's employment.

Health and Medical Journal

Gonorrheal Prostatitis 198

— Dr. Feng Shanliang

After contracting gonorrhea, the gonorrheal diplococcus can invade various parts of the body as acute gonorrhea transitions through subacute gonorrhea to become chronic gonorrhea, often causing complications. When it invades the prostate gland, it causes prostatitis.

The prostate gland is located on both sides of the posterior urethra, between the pubic symphysis and the rectum, and secretes a fluid called prostatic fluid. Its function is to aid the movement of sperm, and it is extremely important for reproductive function. When the gonorrheal diplococcus invades the prostate gland from the posterior urethra, it causes gonorrheal prostatitis as a complication of gonorrhea. Its symptoms can be divided into acute and chronic types.

Acute gonorrheal prostatitis is characterized by severe pain during urination, frequent urination, and even a constant urge to urinate. There is a feeling of pressure in the anus and perineum. Bowel movements cause severe pain in the anus. In severe cases, fever, loss of appetite, and overall pain are experienced. After this period, it gradually becomes chronic gonorrheal prostatitis. At this time, the patient experiences a moderate degree of frequent urination, painful urination, and unusual sensations in the perineum and rectum, often leading to defecation. After suffering from gonorrheal prostatitis, whether acute or chronic, there is a special phenomenon: a milky, turbid secretion often flows from the urethral opening during bowel movements or urination. This is called prostatic leakage. Since prostatic fluid secreted by the prostate gland can aid the movement of sperm, once prostatitis occurs, it will naturally hinder sperm movement. Gonorrheal prostatitis often leads to the inability to have sexual intercourse. Therefore, gonorrheal prostatitis has a very large impact on fertility. If it is not treated promptly and properly, there is a risk of infertility. Treatment should be sought quickly, and the primary goal is to kill the gonococci. At the same time, oral medications should be taken to kill the bacteria. For external medication, Gonorrhea Soother Ear is sure to have great efficacy. In addition, shortwave diathermy is particularly effective, quickly. With shortwave diathermy, the heat can penetrate deeply into the prostate gland and kill the gonococci with heat. The shortwave diathermy treats gonorrhea and all its complications and can achieve results in a short period of time. — Dr. Cui Fuqing

The patient's function is reduced, and a state of increased excitability develops, leading to fatigue, lack of ability, headache, dizziness, insomnia, palpitations, indigestion, back and limb pain, abnormal sensation, and vasomotor disturbances. Excessive Stomach Acid and Stomach Pain 201

— Dr. Liu Xuan

The human stomach is the main organ for digesting food. The stomach constantly secretes a digestive gastric juice containing hydrochloric acid, pepsin, and enzymes. Food enters the stomach through saliva and chewing in the mouth and mixes with gastric juice, causing a fermentation reaction that digests the food. The hydrochloric acid contained in gastric juice has the function of preventing spoilage and killing bacteria. If bacteria are mixed into the stomach due to food, the bacteria's living function can be killed by the action of hydrochloric acid. It also works together with pepsin to convert proteins in food into easily absorbed nutrients, nourishing various parts of the human body. Therefore, gastric acid is extremely important for the body. However, there is a certain amount of acid in the stomach. Both too much and too little can cause disease, especially too much. With excessive stomach acid, the stomach immediately feels pain. The pain is especially severe when the stomach is empty. A burning sensation occurs in the stomach, with symptoms such as acid regurgitation, heartburn, and belching. Because there is too much stomach acid, food is easily digested, so the appetite is particularly good, and the stomach is often hungry. Meat is the easiest to digest, followed by starches. Because stomach acid is very irritating, the gastric mucosa is damaged by excessive irritation from stomach acid, resulting in gastric ulcer disease, which leads to stomach pain. Therefore, those who suffer from hyperacidity often develop stomach ulcers and stomach pain. The most obvious symptom is severe pain in the stomach after eating, often lasting for one or two hours until vomiting occurs. The pain feels burning or spastic. There are often symptoms of heartburn, nausea, belching, and acid regurgitation. Gradually, the stomach bleeds due to the ulcer damaging the blood vessels in the stomach, leading to vomiting of blood and bloody stools. Eventually, gastritis or perforating peritonitis develops, endangering life.

From this, it can be seen that excessive stomach acid is most likely to cause stomach ulcers and stomach pain and will endanger life. It must not be ignored. It has a miraculous effect on neutralizing excessive stomach acid, stopping all stomach pain, and treating all stomach diseases. It is truly a blessing for those with stomach ailments.
